The Recovery of Taihu County, Anhui Province

Anqing Correspondence: Taihu County, Anhui Province, was previously captured by bandits and communists but was soon recovered by the troops of Yan Heling, commander of the 339th Regiment of the 57th Division. Yue Shengxuan, commander of the 57th Division, telegraphed the provincial government yesterday, reporting the recovery process, stating, "I have just received a telegram from Liang, Brigade Commander of my division, relaying a report from Yan Heling, Commander of the 339th Regiment. The report states that I led my troops to advance from Susong to Taihu. At 9 a.m., we arrived at Liangting River and discovered that there were about 2,000 bandits and communists who had captured Taihu at 4 p.m. on the [missing character] day and refused to leave. I then led my troops to continue to advance rapidly. At 11 a.m., we arrived at Maoerling and received a report that the bandits and communists, upon hearing of our army's arrival, were exiting the north gate and fleeing towards Yingshan. At that time, in addition to sending a unit to attack the county via Xiaxia Pass, I led the main force across the mountains via Xiaxia Pass and Jingjie Ridge, bypassing to Lidudian, 20 li northwest of Taihu, to intercept them. We arrived at 8 p.m., but the bandits had already fled. Due to the darkness, it was not convenient to pursue them. I led my troops back to Taihu County to maintain order, etc. In addition to having telegraphed the regiment to remain temporarily in Taihu pending the arrival of Cai's brigade, I respectfully submit this telegram for your information. Yue Shengxuan, Commander of the 57th Division, Hao Wu Can Yin [time notation]." (November 24th)

Transportation in Shandong Province After the War

Actively Restoring Long-Distance Buses and Telephones

Jinan Correspondence: Before the major war this year, Shandong's construction endeavors, such as long-distance buses, were already taking shape. Unfortunately, after the war, all buses were taken away by the military, and the roads were severely damaged. Zhang Honglie, the director of the Construction Department, is actively preparing to restore them. However, although the budget for construction expenses and regular expenses in the 19th fiscal year lists 5,209,600 yuan, the provincial government's finances are difficult, and it can only issue administrative expenses monthly. Business expenses cannot be allocated according to the budget, causing great difficulties for construction projects. Therefore, they have no choice but to start with road administration, requesting and receiving approval from the provincial government to order 25 buses from Shanghai的和記 Company. Once they arrive in early December, they can be distributed to various routes. Currently, the Li-He (Lijin to Heze), De-Lin (Dezhou to Linqing), and Cao-Ji (Caoxian to Jining) routes can still operate. The Dong-Wu (Dongchang to Wuding) route can only be opened after repairs. The Yan-Wei bus route has the largest scale and has not been affected by military activities. However, in fact, this route is controlled by the Yantai area. The remaining routes, such as Jiao-Sha (Jiaozhou to Shazikou) and Ji-Qi (Jinan to Jidong), are all commercially operated. An-Wei (Anqiu to Weixian) is also commercially operated. The province's long-distance telephone system is easier to build because of existing old materials. Eight counties, including Heze, Jiaxiang, Yuncheng, Shanxian, Chengwu, Jinxiang, Juye, and Jining, have been able to make calls and send and receive commercial telegrams since the 15th of this month. The call fee is 2 jiao per 100 li per 5 minutes. The telephone line from Changqing to Feicheng is also about to be completed. Currently, the line from Jinan to Zhangqiu is being installed, and it can be extended to various counties in Jiaodong in the future. As for the Xiaqing River, the only waterway in the province, the Construction Department is also planning to dredge it to allow small steamers to pass. Due to financial difficulties, it is proposed to ask Chairman Han to allocate the Third Route Engineering Corps to assist in order to expedite the process. (November 26th)

Chen Jitang's Winter Defense Conference After Returning to Guangdong

Six Concrete Measures for Winter Defense Decided

The city is divided and assigned to military police and police

Scheduled to be implemented on December 15th

Guangzhou Correspondence: Winter defense is approaching, and the provincial and municipal authorities are paying close attention to this issue. Chen Jitang, commander-in-chief of the Eighth Route Army, returned to Guangdong this time not only to discuss Zhang Gui's surrender but also to arrange winter defense matters in the province. On the evening of the 20th of this month, Chen convened a winter defense conference at the headquarters to discuss winter defense arrangements. In Guangzhou, the execution is entrusted to the military police and the Public Security Bureau, while in other areas, it is jointly responsible by the defense army county soldiers, and local militias. The navy will send fleets to patrol each river section for defense. The suburbs of Guangzhou City will be defended by He Fangbin's troops of the 126th Brigade. After receiving the order, He's troops have been preparing for days to move the entire four battalions to Xiaogang, Sanyuanli, Tangxi, Tangxia, Tangyong, and other places north of the city, selecting sites for stationing. The military police headquarters has formed a special patrol team, dividing the urban area into segments for patrols day and night. The Public Security Bureau also drafted six winter defense measures on the 19th and distributed them to each Public Security Bureau branch for implementation. The specific measures are: (1) Order the Detective Section to select capable detectives to be stationed in each branch to assist in investigating petty thieves on a regular basis, with two assigned to each bureau. (2) Order each branch to suspend police drills during the winter defense period to focus on duty. (3) Issue a notice to increase the number of off-duty police officers to organize armed police patrol teams, all equipped with rifles, ready to patrol the streets at any time. (4) Resume inspection of gun permits. Each branch will set its own time to send police teams to important locations on each street to check pedestrians and vehicles to prevent petty thieves from mingling. (5) Search suspicious households. For mixed-residence areas and suspicious households where many strangers enter and exit within each branch's jurisdiction, the police should be sent to search at any time. If it is found that the population does not match the household registration, they should be detained for questioning. (6) Order the Haizhu, Nantoutou, and Etan branches to carefully inspect boats anchored in the provincial river and prohibit sand boats from lodging guests. After the above measures are implemented, the security of the suburbs will be jointly defended by the bureau in conjunction with the Nanfan County guard team. The authorities have scheduled the winter defense measures to be implemented by military and police agencies starting on December 15th. (November 22nd)

Through Train from Beijing to Liaoning Starts from Shenyang

Shenyang Correspondence: The Ministry of Railways has ordered the Jinpu and Beining Railway Bureaus to be responsible for preparing for the through train from Beijing to Liaoning, which is scheduled to start operating on the 24th of this month. The two bureaus have reached a compromise and will each provide a train set. Every Monday and Thursday, trains will depart from Pukou to Shenyang. Every Monday and Friday, trains will depart from Shenyang to Pukou. There will be a total of four round trips per week. The journey time is approximately 65 hours. The first train departed from Shenyang at 0:10 a.m. today (the 24th). Before the opening of the train service, the Tianjin General Bureau of the Beining Railway assigned the train, with a total of 13 cars including the locomotive. In addition to the baggage car and guard car allocated by the HuangguTun car factory, the remaining nine cars were attached to Pan on the 22nd and 23rd. The Shenyang office was notified to prepare the vehicles by noon on the 24th. In order to facilitate the transportation of mail, the Liaoning Postal Administration also began to scan the train service times on the same day. All express mail destined for the Jinpu Line and transferred from Jinpu to other places will be transported by the Beijing-Liaoning through train, with a special mail car attached to the rear of the train. Before 10 p.m. on the 23rd, the train drove from HuangguTun to Shenyang City Station to wait for the departure time. Because it was the first train, few people knew about it, so the train was not very crowded. (November 24th)

Yanbian Requests to Increase Police

Korean Bandits Rampant

Shenyang Correspondence: The Yanji Federation of Agriculture, Industry, Commerce, and Education previously sent an express mail telegram to the Northeast officials requesting more police. The telegram read as follows: "Yanbian is unfortunately on the Japanese chopping block, suffering unspeakable pain. Recently, we requested the withdrawal of the police, which was unanimously agreed upon nationwide, and the Japanese could hardly refuse. However, on the 4th, all the police were withdrawn in the middle of the night. Korean bandits took the opportunity to become rampant, disrupting the area. The hard work of Yanbian farmers over the years has been reduced to ashes. Life and property are precarious. If we do not take measures to stop them, I am afraid that not only will the border people suffer, but it will also give people an excuse [to interfere]. If you do not consider the border people to be uncivilized, I implore you to increase the police as soon as possible to suppress the chaos." At the same time, the Liaoning National Diplomacy Association also received an appeal from the Yanji agricultural, industrial, commercial, and educational groups, requesting support. In addition to sending a telegram to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee and the Jilin Provincial Government to plead for Yanji, the association's entire committee also met with Zhang Zuoxiang, chairman of Jilin Province and acting chairman of the Political Affairs Committee, to promote the implementation. The telegram stated, "We have just received a telegram from the Yanji Federation of Agriculture, Industry, Commerce, and Education stating that since the Japanese freely increased the police last month, the border people have suffered unspeakable pain. Although they have now been withdrawn, Korean bandits are rampant, killing and setting fires, disrupting the area, and the lives and property of the border people are precarious. They have no choice but to send a telegram to the Northeast officials requesting more police. We hope you will assist in implementing this. Yanji is the throat of the Northeast and an important national defense area. The mixing of Chinese and foreigners makes the situation even more complicated. If more police are not deployed, not only will the residents of the area not have security, but governance will also fall into the hands of foreigners. We implore your committee to quickly raise funds and increase the number of police by a specific date to protect the people and defend the country."

Wuhu Quick News

Wuhu's Fifth and Twenty-sixth Rear Hospitals currently have approximately one thousand several hundred wounded soldiers, but they have almost fully recovered. The Headquarters Wounded Soldier Management Committee dispatched five members to Wuhu yesterday to inspect everything and plans to close the two hospitals. Also, Zhang Zhizhong, the commander of the Second Training Division, sent staff member Zhang Wenxin to Wuhu yesterday to investigate the wounded soldiers of the division and give 10 yuan to each officer and 3 yuan to each soldier as consolation.

The establishment of a rice market preparation office in the capital caused Anhui merchants to fear that the Wuhu rice market would be relocated. They repeatedly telegraphed the National Government and all parties to appeal. Recently, they received an order from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stating that the establishment of a rice market in Nanjing is a plan of the Capital Construction Committee and has been filed with the National Government. There is no intention to move the Wuhu rice market to Beijing. The two are parallel and do not conflict. There is no need to abolish the capital rice market.

Previously, wounded soldier Lin Debiao openly robbed a person at the Shenghequan bathhouse in Dongmen. The Sixth District Bandit Suppression Command sent a team to capture him on the spot. According to an order from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, he will be tied to the Thirteen Gates this afternoon at 2 p.m. and executed by firing squad to serve as a warning.

The Anhui Finance Department Special Commissioner's Office moved from Wuhu back to the old water police station in Anqing. All personnel, documents, and furniture were transported by special ship yesterday. It was decided to officially open the office in the province on the 27th. A Wuhu office will be established and managed by Ye Qize, the director of the sugar tax bureau. The bureau will be moved to the Henan Special Commissioner's Office.

The County Party Department held a Party Ideology speech contest for all levels of schools in Wuhu at the Second Women's Normal School yesterday. Fifteen male and female students from secondary schools and more than twenty students from primary schools participated. The provincial government chairman and members all provided shields, books, and other awards. As a result, Feng Debiao from the secondary school group and Huang Yanhua from the primary school group won first place and were awarded by Zhao Jingshi, the director of the Public Security Bureau.

The bandits and communists in the Langxi and Guangde areas of southern Anhui are eager to make trouble. After the entire regiment of Yu Fengrun of the 57th Division was dispatched, the bandits and communists went into hiding. The regiment is currently searching in various ways. Now that winter defense has arrived in the three counties of Wuhu, Xuancheng, and Dangtu, joint defense is extremely important. The county magistrates of the three counties personally led their self-defense corps to the Huangchi Town assembly point in Dangtu yesterday, with a total of approximately 400 corps police. In the future, assemblies will be held once a month to facilitate communication. (25th)

Zhenjiang Quick News

The Provincial Party Rectification Committee has appointed the following county party rectification committee members: Wang Cheng of Yizheng, Yin Muzhou of Gaochun (due to inability to take office, Yin Yuhua was appointed as a replacement), Wang Yueping of Nanhui (dismissed and replaced by Pan Hui), Jiang Yuan of Danyang (transferred back, Zuo Yuanbai designated as兼 Minister of Organization), Xin Yutang of Pixian (transferred back, Yin Zhenhuai appointed as a replacement), Wang Liping of Shanghai (dismissed).

The first section of Zhongzheng Road in the provincial capital, from the South Gate Station to Dashikou, has been completed. The provincial government telegraphed the Ministry of Railways yesterday, specially ordering the railway bureau to have all trains stop at the South Gate Station starting from December 1st to facilitate travel.

Construction of the Zhenjiang-Guangde Road, Zhenjiang-Danyang section, is scheduled to begin on December 1st. The first district of this county has telegraphed the town chiefs of each township to rush the creation of a conscription roster.

The second administrative meeting of Zhenjiang County opened at 2 p.m. yesterday, presided over by County Magistrate Zhang Peng. Leng Yu was publicly elected as vice chairman. Members of the proposal review committee were designated. The meeting will last for three days.

The Public Security Bureau recently cracked the kidnapping case of Wang Zhiyuan's family in Jianbi, capturing the main culprits Mao Peihua and others, a total of thirteen people, who have been transferred to the Security Department for interrogation. The other suspects, Zuo Liangfu, Jiang Zhang, Chen Qi, Wu Gao, Wang Liu, Xu Liangtian, Liu Zhushan, Ma Wu, Zhu Faming, Wang Xingyi, Ma Qian, and Su Zhuang, a total of twelve people, were questioned and found to be unrelated and will be released on bail.

Dingfengyong Silk Factory has suspended production again due to a shortage of cocoon supply.

The singer Cai Changchun lost the case for demanding marital autonomy.

Local Correspondence

Nanhui

Joint Defense of Three Counties to be Held Soon The joint defense of Fengxian, Nanhui, and Chuansha counties was previously decided at a meeting of the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs. Now, the three counties have consulted on the implementation method and decided that Nanhui will send 16 police officers, Fengxian will send 12 police officers, and Chuansha will send 8 police officers, with one captain in charge of command. The joint defense team will be organized soon to maintain local security.

Expand the Police Force to Raise Operating Expenses The police force of this county has always been one company (one company consists of three platoons). Now, due to defense needs, it has been decided to add one platoon. The operating expenses will be raised by the county by formulating a donation roster and distributing it to various districts for active solicitation. All funds must be raised and submitted to the county within one month to expedite the opening.

Qingpu

Change of County Public Security Bureau Director The current County Public Security Bureau Director Zhu Hua has been in office for two years. It is said that the provincial government has decided to transfer Zhu Hua to be the director of the Suining County Public Security Bureau, and the vacancy will be filled by Shen Jinghua, the current director of the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau.

The City God Idols Completely Destroyed The City God Temple in this county has always been very popular. Previously, the various agencies in the city, in order to break superstitions, had all the staff members go to the temple with weapons the night before and destroyed all 82 idols, large and small, leaving only the statue of Shen Gong, which was placed in a separate room as a special ancestral hall.

Songjiang

Shatian Bureau Measures and Releases Zhangze and Yexie Official Wasteland The Songjiang Jinqing Shatian Official Property Office, in the Zhangze and Yexie areas of Songjiang, such as Yantie Village, Nanxin Village, Yuanjia Village, etc., has many food-free official wasteland base areas. Some have been measured but not released, or have not yet been measured. It is now planned to send personnel to the countryside to start measuring in order to allow the official wasteland to be claimed and the grain to be paid as soon as possible to increase tax revenue. However, at the beginning of the process, it is feared that the local villagers are ignorant or may misunderstand. It is planned to issue a joint announcement from the county bureau and submit it to the county government for approval and printing.

Convene Township Chiefs to Review Budgets and Final Accounts The county government believes that the budgets and final accounts submitted by various districts are not satisfactory. After discussing the methods at the county political meeting, it is necessary to convene district affairs meetings to review them. Each member must be responsible for signing and sealing the documents. In the future, funds not listed in the budget must be approved before they can be used. The preliminary budget and final accounts of the first district office have been prepared and sent to the township chiefs of each township for review to avoid being rushed at the last minute and unable to review in detail. Yesterday (27th), a district affairs meeting was convened to discuss the budget for this year. It was said that the estimated income from land rent seemed too large and was slightly reduced. The annual calculation book was reviewed item by item according to the vouchers. All expenses were found to be legitimate. A review report was prepared accordingly and sealed by all the members present, and it was submitted immediately.

Fellow Townsmen in Yangzhou Request the Pursuit of Former Magistrate Wen's Debt There are still many Songjiang County public funds that were owed by the former county magistrate due to unclearly handed over responsibilities, especially the 150,000 owed by Wen Shaoliang during the Luqi War in the thirteenth year, which is the largest amount. Now, An Shisui, Wang Zihou, Wang Wei, Sun Shiheng, Xu Weiji, and other fellow townsmen from Songjiang residing in Yangzhou, upon seeing the news that the Zhejiang Provincial Government was planning to re-employ him, telegraphed Beijing and the province the day before yesterday, stating, "Wen Shaoliang, the former county magistrate of Songjiang County, owed public funds and failed to hand them over. The Provincial Government's 292nd meeting has already decided to issue a warrant for his arrest to maintain official discipline and clear the backlog of cases. However, we have seen reports that Wen Shaoliang has recently been appointed as the county magistrate by the Zhejiang Provincial Government. The Zhejiang Provincial Government may not be aware of the Jiangsu Province's arrest warrant for Wen, and Wen is greedy and insatiable. The future of the party and the country is extremely worrying. We, Shisui, etc., are heartbroken and cannot remain silent. We request that you transfer the case to the Zhejiang Provincial Government and immediately remove the newly appointed County Magistrate Wen Shaoliang from office, place him under supervision, and hand him over for strict punishment. The future of the party and the country depends on this."

Suzhou

The Danger of Infectious Diseases in the Third Prison of Xiaoliuzhen Lane The Third Prison of Jiangsu, originally an old prison, has a fixed quota of 500 prisoners, but the number has now more than doubled, with more than 1,300 prisoners. Recently, in November, dysentery and infectious diseases were suddenly discovered among the prisoners. More than 30 people have died this month alone. Lin, President of the Higher Court, fearing the spread of infectious diseases among the prisoners, which would be uncontrollable, and concerned about the lives of the prisoners, specially appointed Jail Division Chief Yao Guozhang on the afternoon of the 26th to go to the prison to investigate the cause of the prisoners' illness and find ways to remedy it. Fortunately, when Yao went to investigate, a prisoner had just died. It was found that as many as 49 prisoners in the entire prison were suffering from this infectious disease, including five who were most in danger and likely to die. Yao immediately ordered Warden Cai to call Chinese and Western doctors to the prison for diagnosis and treatment, ordering them to find ways to isolate the patients and return to the court to report. After receiving the report, Lin was very anxious and prepared to submit a report to the Ministry of Justice, requesting the Ministry to transfer it to the court for review and approval of the method of pardoning prisoners based on the resolutions of the Fourth Plenary Session at the New Year's Day of the 20th year of the Republic of China in order to relieve prison overcrowding and benefit the lives of the prisoners.

Haimen Trial Judge Accused of Taking Bribes to Release Prisoners A Haimen County trial judge was accused of taking bribes to release sentenced prisoners Liu Sanlang and others. Yesterday, citizens of the county telegraphed the Higher Court requesting investigation and punishment. After receiving the report, the Higher Court had the prosecutor's office review it.

Robbers Shot and Killed Farmers Residents of Changsha Village, Shiba Du, San Tu, Xiangshan Township, in the county, Yu [missing character]bao's house, was suddenly robbed by seven or eight robbers the day before yesterday, suffering heavy losses. When the robbers were leaving, they encountered a villager, Yu Fusheng, carrying firewood on his shoulders at Nanwang Bridge. The robbers opened fire and shot Fusheng in the chest, with more than ten wounds. Fusheng died of his injuries at about 3 p.m. that afternoon. Afterwards, the victim reported the incident to the Second Resident Station of the Ninth Branch for investigation.

Local Ruffians Extort Villagers Chen Jinyuan, a villager from Shiqian Village, Chenmu Township, in the county, had a love affair with the widow Gu Wang. Liao Hongyi, a ruffian in the town, colluded with Town Chief Wang Songyan to extort 746 yuan from Chen and gave 150 yuan to a certain organization in the town. After someone tipped off the Public Security Bureau, Director Zou ordered Qian Peng, director of the Fifteenth Branch, to investigate. Director Qian submitted a reply yesterday, stating that the case was privately mediated by town gentry Zou Xiwu, Wang Zeyi, and others at the district office. After receiving the reply, Director Zou ordered Director Qian yesterday to detain all the witnesses in the case for investigation.

Rice Shop Owner Commits Suicide Due to Debt Shen Gengyu, the owner of Shen Guangcheng Rice Shop in Jiaozhi, committed suicide with a handgun at the Chamber of Commerce (Shen was a member) on the 25th due to business failure and debt of more than 10,000 yuan. On the 27th, Prosecutor Lu was sent by the local court for inspection.

Wuxi

Robbery and Murder on a Boat, Shooting of a Villager:

At the junction of Wuxi and Changshu, near Xueyan Bridge, in the Minjiaqiao area, a villager named Gao Chanlin, over sixty years old, went to the city with a fellow villager (some say his son) the day before yesterday. They rented an open boat, intending to transport thatch to the city for sale. Yesterday, around eleven o'clock, as the boat was sailing in the Shaotangying area (about twelve or thirteen li from Xueyan Bridge), three bandits suddenly appeared on the shore. They spoke with a northern accent, wore tattered uniforms, and carried two rifles. The lead bandit ordered them to stop the boat. Chanlin was sitting at the bow, smoking a cigarette, when the bandits, without asking questions, aimed their rifles at the flickering cigarette and fired. With a loud bang, Chanlin was shot and fell, dying instantly. The bullet entered through Chanlin's eye socket and exited from the back of his head. His companion, witnessing the scene, was terrified and, fearing for his life, docked the boat. The three bandits jumped aboard, searched the boat thoroughly, and found nothing. They then robbed Chanlin's companion of fifteen silver dollars, which he had hidden, and fled. Afterwards, the local villagers reported the incident to the county, requesting an investigation. It is also reported that the Seventeenth District Office, together with the Fourteenth Branch Bureau police, have apprehended three bandits.

Request to Postpone the Issuance of Construction Bonds:

The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce believes that the Jiangsu Provincial Government's issuance of the first phase of construction bonds, totaling four million yuan, with Wuxi being allocated two hundred thousand yuan, is disproportionately high. In recent years, various industries have been repeatedly ordered to raise funds for various bonds, leaving them utterly depleted. Bonds, paid at ninety-eight percent of their face value, often only fetch fifty to sixty percent of their original value in the Shanghai market, resulting in hidden losses borne by merchants. This construction bond is specifically designated to be repaid with funds from the real estate deed tax, but this year, due to low grain prices harming farmers and reduced land sales, except in a few cities, income has greatly decreased, taxes have doubled, prices have fallen daily, and there are few transactions. Whether the deed tax will continue to be robust in the future is questionable. Furthermore, the silk market is declining, causing a sharp drop in the market, and with the year-end closing approaching, many businesses rely on relief and find it extremely difficult to meet their obligations. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Provincial Government Finance Department, and Construction Department of the National Government in Nanjing, requesting them to consider the people's hardship and temporarily postpone the issuance of Jiangsu's construction bonds to ease the burden on the people.

Shen Changyuan Rice Shop Nearly Bankrupt:

The Qingyang Shen Changyuan Rice Shop in Jiangyin County, which has been established for many years and has an excellent reputation, is in danger of bankruptcy. The owner, Shen Jinqing, once served as a court official in the township but faced accusations of embezzlement due to financial issues. Shen is skilled in maneuvering. During the time when the old warlord Qi Xieyuan served as the Jiangsu military governor, Shen became acquainted with Qi's quartermaster. All military rice purchases for Qi's troops were handled solely by Shen, resulting in significant profits. Shen Jinqing's son, Wenhua, opened the Wenji Gold Shop in Shanghai with Liu Tichen, a fellow townsman, last year. However, managing gold was not their forte, and they suffered heavy losses, amounting to over two hundred seventy thousand yuan, forcing them to close the gold shop. The large sums of money owed by Wenhua were mostly dragged from Shanghai and Suzhou banks. Consequently, his father's Shen Changyuan Rice Shop also nearly went bankrupt. The Shanghai and Suzhou financial circles have also been greatly affected. It is rumored that the Shui Hengfeng Bank in this city lost about fifty to sixty thousand gold, and the Rui Yingrun Bank also lost more than thirty thousand yuan.

Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Xiyi Provincial Road:

The Xiyi Provincial Road, since being actively prepared by Yao Dixing, the head of the County Construction Bureau, is now ready. The Construction Department has approved the commencement of construction on December 1st. Director Yao has also scheduled the groundbreaking ceremony to be held at the south end of Meiyuan at 2:00 PM on the same day.

Successive Extortion Letters from Bandits:

Recently, robberies have become rampant in the surrounding villages. Although the authorities have been working hard to apprehend the bandits, it has been difficult to eradicate them completely. Recently, Shen Jinhua, the owner of Demao Sen Silk Shop outside the North Gate, received a threatening letter from bandits demanding fifty thousand yuan. The other day, Zhang Heqing, the owner of Kunhe Tin Shop on Beida Street, suddenly received a threatening letter, stating that because the army lacks funds, they were borrowing three thousand silver dollars for their use. After reading the letter, Zhang Heqing ignored it.

Change of District Chiefs in County Government:

Shen Guoliang, the District Chief of the Ninth District of Wu County, resigned after being appointed as the General Affairs Section Chief of the Education Bureau. His resignation was approved by the County Government yesterday (the 26th). Cheng Fuyu, the District Chief of the Fourth District, was appointed as the District Chief of the Ninth District. The vacancy of District Chief of the Fourth District was filled by Liu Baorun, who had previously served as the District Chief of that area. The officials will transfer their duties separately within the next few days.

Change of Two Judges in County Court:

Xue Guang, a judge of the Criminal Court of Wu County Court, was appointed as a judge of the First Branch of the Qingjiang Higher Court yesterday by the Higher Court. The vacancy was filled by Ling Yizhong, the former chief clerk of the court. Tong Jianmo, a judge of the Civil Court, was ordered to switch positions with Chai Zupeng, a judge of the Nantong County Court.

Further Apprehension of Bandits in Bridge Robbery Case:

In the case of robberies at the homes of Fan Shui and others in Luqiao Town, Sixth District of Wu County, the detective team of the Public Security Bureau previously apprehended two bandits, Mei Xiaomou and Wang Heshang. Yu Rong, the director of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, recently received a report from the victims stating that another bandit, Zhou Zimou, was hiding in Xuju Village. They went to apprehend him on the 25th. After a clear preliminary hearing, he was sent to the County Court for questioning on the 26th.

Jiangyin

Yun Ting Security Corps Captures Four Bandits:

The Yun Ting Security Corps, after discovering that bandits were meeting at Yangtou Mountain late at night, dispatched over forty militiamen led by Drillmaster Tu to surround them. Upon arriving at Yangtou Mountain, they found no activity and continued their search. They moved past Batou Mountain to Shanzhuang Shang Village, where bandits were indeed holding a meeting. Contact was made, and gunfire was exchanged. The militiamen captured five bandits, while one escaped. They also seized over a hundred rounds of ammunition, leather goods, clothing, and other stolen items. They will be sent to the county for interrogation in the coming days.

Three Farmhouses Robbed in One Night:

Ren Genxi, a farmer in the Sanguan Township of the Second District, was relatively well-off. At 9:00 PM on the 25th, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived to rob his home, stealing clothing and foreign currency worth hundreds of yuan. Before leaving, they demanded another two hundred yuan within three days. A similar robbery occurred at the nearby home of Li Yuzhou in Jiangjiaqiao, with minor losses. More than ten bandits also arrived at Wu Balang's home in Guanzhuang. Because they did not find any clothing or foreign currency, they threatened to contact him secretly within three days, and dared not to speak out.

The Urban Area Security Corps cracked down on a Communist Party organ in the east wing, arresting Huang Jinlin, Gao Hong, Xu Mengshi, and others. Huang confessed to serving as a Communist Party member. Gao Hong and others had joined in robberies. On the 26th, they were transferred to the Qingxiang Bureau and then to the Provincial Government Military Tribunal for interrogation.

Liu Boyang, the director of the Business Tax Collection Registration Office in Tongyi, came to Tongzhou from the province to work in the Finance Bureau. Chen Zhilin and others have been appointed as clerks. Cheng Chunyi, chairman of the General Chamber of Commerce, has been hired as a consultant.

With the opening of Yao Port in Tongyi, the Tuozhu Road from the city to the port is under construction. The Construction Bureau has submitted a request to the provincial and county governments, and work is scheduled to begin on December 1st.

Various industries in Nantong will close their accounts for both local and out-of-town receivables and payables at the end of the lunar year.

Rugao

Arrest of Key Figures Leading Resistance to Donations:

Xue Shaoheng and others, wealthy households in Chema Lake, were arrested for organizing a public march to protest the security corps donation, resulting in security corps members firing shots and injuring people. Yesterday, the police squadron stationed in Che County, upon the order of the battalion commander, arrested Xue Shaoheng, Xue Huiwu, Jiang Tong, and three others who instigated the resistance, and sent them for interrogation.

Major Bandits Arrested in Shanghai One After Another:

The Rugao County Government previously dispatched detective team leader Guo and team members Wang Side and others to Shanghai to apprehend bandit Xu. Within less than ten days, they captured major bandit Shi Maofei. Team leader Guo personally escorted him back. Wang and others remained in Shanghai to investigate and apprehend other key bandits. Later, at the Changyuan Pig Shop in the Bund, they captured major bandit Li Zhongru. They reported this to the police for assistance. The bandit cunningly denied his identity, claiming to be Ding Xiaofu. The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau temporarily detained him and inquired with the county government about the situation. Upon receiving the letter, the county government prepared a document and dispatched police officers to Shanghai on this day (the 24th) to escort the bandit back.

Yangzhou

Population Census to Be Completed Within One Month:

The County Government, upon receiving instructions from the Civil Affairs Department, announced that the provincial population census will begin on December 1st and must be completed within one month. The county is instructed to follow the instructions, complete the census on time, prepare various statistical tables, and submit them for review. Yesterday (the 25th), the County Government instructed all district offices to comply.

Brigade Commander Yan Escorted to Provincial Security Department:

The 133rd Brigade stationed in Yangzhou, together with the Police Brigade and Public Security Bureau, detained Yan Hanchen (also known as Yan Zhaofeng), as well as Wang Fuheng, Zhang Zhenhua, Ding Yuhua, Zhu Hesheng, Zhu Xingchun, and Li Wenqing. They also seized seals, appointment certificates, symbols, and more from previous years. It is said that the brigade headquarters had previously issued a notice prohibiting the recruitment of soldiers, but Yan Zhaofeng dared to impersonate a brigade commander, appoint personnel, and recruit bandits, plotting illegal activities, which is a violation of the law. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 26th, he was transported across the river by car and handed over to the Provincial Security Department for investigation.

Warden on the Run, Medical Officer Arrested:

Chen Quan, the warden of the Jiangdu Detention Center, was dismissed due to a prison break case and is awaiting trial. It was reported that the Zhenjiang District Court of the High Court ordered Chen Quan to be tried, but Chen Quan had been released on bail for 500 yuan for medical treatment. The court summoned him previously, but only Chief Zhu and guards attended. It is now learned that Chen did not appear on the court date of the 20th (Second Tribunal). The County Court arrested Wang Yuchun, the medical officer of the detention center who vouched for Chen.

Wang confessed that he vouched for Chen out of colleagueship. Yesterday (the 25th), the court detained Wang and requested an arrest warrant for Chen Quan.

Huangjue Bridge Robbery Case:

In Huangjue Bridge Shangshui City, in the domain of this city, a banditry happened at a resident Wang Hantian's house. On the afternoon of the other day (24th) at 8 o'clock, suddenly a dozen bandits came. Among them, two had box guns, first climbed the wall and entered, opening the door to let the rest of the bandits in. It happened that Wang was not at home, so they tortured his wife to force her to hand over valuables. It is heard that clothes, jewelry and silver dollars, totaling about hundreds of yuan, were lost. After the bandits left, the family immediately reported to the 10th Public Security Branch, and forwarded to the main bureau to request an arrest warrant.

Court Investigates Sudden Death of Woman:

In Dengcao Lane, Wanzi Street, in the main city, at the house of Chen Hanwen, a tooth merchant, (Chen lived here alone) yesterday, a woman from Shaobo came to Yangzhou and was staying at Chen's house. When she first arrived, she only said she had a headache, but unexpectedly she died in bed this morning. Chen, seeing this, told his neighbors that he was going out to look for the woman's family to come and collect her body. Chen Hanwen did not return until 4:00 PM in the afternoon. Therefore, the neighbors reported the incident to the County Court, and the prosecutor went to the scene to investigate. After the investigation, the coffin was ordered to be prepared and sealed first, and Chen Hanwen was summoned to the case to investigate the cause of the woman's death and the relationship between Chen and the woman.

Adultery with Sister-in-Law, Eyes Gouged Out:

In Bao Lane Village, south of Ganquan Mountain in this county, there was a farmer named Xu Xiyuan, who had two sons, Bao Hong and Bao Jiang. The eldest son married a woman named Chen, who had an affair with the younger son, Bao Jiang, and considered Bao Hong an eyesore. Therefore, she sowed discord with his father, stating various illegal acts of Bao Hong. The other day, the brothers agreed to reason with each other at the house of their uncle, Shao Shaonian. On the way, in the Beishuangshan area, Bao Jiang had people ambushed in advance. The eyes of Bao Hong were gouged out and blinded with lime. Now, neighbors are speaking out on his behalf and plan to file a complaint with the court.

Gaoyou

Shooting Accident Leads to Death in Town:

Cai Hongbin, a bugler in the Gao Bao You Patrol Team stationed at the Guandi Temple on the South Gate Yunti, was chatting with his friend Le Gengcheng the other day. Le saw that Cai was wearing a box gun, so he took it in his hand to play with it. Unexpectedly, he touched the trigger, and with a bang, a bullet was fired, hitting Cai's vital point. He fell to the ground. After many people mediated, Le paid for Cai to be sent to the Zhenjiang Hospital for treatment. It is now heard that he has died due to his serious injuries. The Gao Bao You Patrol Team has first detained Le and is waiting for the deceased's family to come to You to handle the matter.

Feng Family Robbed in Zhuma Village:

The home of Feng Baochu, a farmer in Zhuma Village, Huxi County, was robbed the other night by a group of bandits. They ransacked the house, stealing a self-defense gun, over two hundred bullets, dozens of dan of rice, clothing, silver dollars, and other items, resulting in significant losses.

Pinghu

New Tricks of Recruitment Committee:

Wang Wenzhao, the former recruitment committee member stationed at the Great King Temple outside the East Gate of Pinghu, has been lingering in the same place despite the central government's abolition of the recruitment agencies. At the Yongkang Bridge outside the East Gate, Wang was holding a small glass bottle, pretending to collide with a pedestrian, Mr. Wu, and smashing it, claiming that the bottle contained a special medicine for illness, worth over a hundred gold, which was entrusted to him by his superiors, so it must be compensated in full. As a result, Wu was swindled out of four yuan. Later, near the telephone company on Xiaojie Street, he used the same trick to defraud a passerby of six yuan. The authorities soon learned of this and went to investigate. Wang escaped after hearing the news. It is also learned that before Wang fled, he had sent a letter to Zhang Pinghou, who operates a rice business, borrowing ten yuan, but fortunately it was not delivered.

Two Cases of Extortion by Bandits in Xin Cang:

Zhu Jinrong, a villager in Shijiaodang, about three li from Xincang, is quite wealthy. The other day, bandit leader Liu De led more than ten bandits to Zhu's house to extort money. Jinrong was out, so Zhu's son came out to negotiate. The bandits demanded three thousand yuan, to be delivered within three days. Later, they went to the house of Tang Erdi, who blows and beats instruments for a living in Xia Liqiaonan. Erdi was holding a small child. The bandits took the child away, intending to extort a ransom. Eventually, after someone intervened, the child was returned, but they demanded one thousand yuan, also to be paid within three days. If not fulfilled, they would burn down the house.

Hangzhou

Public Memorial Service for Wu Changshuo by Members of the Seal Society:

Wu Changshuo, a gold and stone artist from Shanghai, was a member of the Xiling Society in Hangzhou. Now, the members of the society, lamenting that his death in Shanghai has resulted in the extinction of a true master of his generation, have deeply regretted it. His son has chosen a burial site in Chaoshan for his father. The coffin has already been transported there. Thirty members of the Seal Society, including Wang Lengzhou, Ruan Xingshan, and Jin Hequan, regretted not attending the funeral in Shanghai, so they held a public memorial service yesterday to pay their respects.

Lottery for Sorting Out Old Debts and Public Bonds:

Yesterday, the Finance Department held the ninth lottery for sorting out old debts and public bonds at the City Chamber of Commerce. Ten tickets were drawn, and the numbers were 14, 08, 25, 33, 52, 54, 66, 77, 86, and 94. Principal and interest will begin to be repaid on the second of next month. If the funds are insufficient, the Finance Department will provide them.

Jiangxi Bandits Rise Again, Zhejiang Troops Strictly Defend:

Yesterday it was learned that two groups of Jiangxi bandits, Fang and Shao, are being thoroughly suppressed by troops dispatched by Shandong Province, and have fled to the vicinity of Shangrao. The 3rd regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team stationed on the border of Jiangxi, upon hearing the news, specially dispatched teams to strictly defend the counties of Jiang and Chang. The provincial government has received an urgent telegram from the Jiangxi provincial government informing them of this.

Shaoxing

Chief of Keqiao Public Security Bureau Flees in Fear of Punishment:

Wang Tongkui, the chief of the Keqiao Public Security Bureau in Shaoxing, has been accused of abusing his power and harming the people in the Keqiao fire case. The victim, Sun Zonghai, has filed a complaint with the provincial government and the local branch court. The provincial government has ordered the Shaoxing county to suspend him from his duties for investigation. Wang, fearing punishment, abandoned his post and fled on the afternoon of the 25th. Upon receiving the news, the Public Security Bureau sent personnel to take over his duties and requested an arrest warrant.

Robbery in Xixiang Houshe:

A robbery occurred at the home of Yu Dexin in Xixiang Houshe, Shaoxing, on the night of the 25th. The losses are significant. The victim has reported the incident to the authorities and requested an arrest.

Xiaoshan

Kidnapping and Ransom Case in Kanshan Town:

At around 10:00 PM on the 24th, five bandits broke into the Fang Jia Yan house in Houfang Village, Kanshan, eastern Xiaoshan, robbed the house, and kidnapped the owner. The bandits fled towards Shaoxing County and left a letter, stating that they were passing through Ningbo and needed food and supplies, requesting a loan of 50,000 yuan.

Dike Association Levies Donations, Telegram to Province Calling for Help:

Representatives of merchants and residents of the entire Shangshanhe Town in Xiaoshan, including all the merchants, sent a telegram to the province, county, and central government, stating that the Hechang Da Sanxiang Flood Control Association had illegally levied 680 yuan from the shops in Heshanzhen Yangshu, demanding payment by a deadline, otherwise they would be arrested. They requested redress. The provincial government has ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau and the county government to thoroughly investigate the case.

Shangyu

Sheng Bandits Invade Again, Many Killed:

The southern border of Yu County has been disturbed by a large group of Sheng bandits since late last month. After the security teams of various counties joined forces to fight them, the bandits retreated to Chongren County in Sheng County. However, in the middle of this month, the bandits learned that the security teams had returned to their original defenses, so they returned and passed through Huangzhai, where they were ambushed by the local security forces, killing forty-three bandits. The remaining bandits fled in three directions: one retreated to the old nest of Chongren, one fled to Tangtian Dongcun, kidnapping the owner of a certain hotel and a man known as Gan Zhulao, and one fled to Dingxia Town, kidnapping the resident Yuanhe. Security corps in the affected areas have stepped up patrols and are on alert day and night.

Wang Zhengui Robbed at Feast:

Wang Zhengui, the deputy chief of Wangjiahui Village in the west of the county, held a feast for his grandson's first birthday. After the feast, a group of more than ten guests were playing mahjong when, at around 10:00 PM, eight bandits suddenly broke in, each holding a wooden toy gun. One bandit stood guard outside the door, four bandits restrained the gamblers, and three bandits went upstairs to search for valuables. They looted more than forty silver dollars and over twenty silver dollars worth of jewelry before leaving towards Sanjie.

Important News

President Zhu Jiahua of Zhongda Returns to Guangdong Yesterday

To Handle Matters at Sun Yat-sen University

Will Return to Beijing in Three Weeks to Take Office

Nanjing, 27th - Zhu Jiahua told reporters that he has been in charge of Sun Yat-sen University for a short time. The school's projects are well underway, and the salaries of the colleagues are relatively low. They were invited based on personal relationships and are willing to sacrifice for the cause. He heard nothing about his transfer to Zhongda beforehand. Since it has been announced, it is not appropriate to refuse, as it would break administrative faith. He is leaving for Guangdong tonight to handle the handover and explain everything to his colleagues so that they can be at ease with their duties. When asked about his plans to improve Zhongda, Zhu replied that he is not yet familiar with Zhongda's internal situation and organization, so he cannot talk about improvement plans at this time.

Jiangsu Education Funds Should Be Planned Quickly

Letter from the Education Funds Management Office to the Education Funds Committee

Income and Expenses Fall Short by More Than 1.58 Million Yuan

A letter from the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office to the Jiangsu Education Funds Committee stated:

Respectfully, in the past, in order to raise and distribute funds to various schools, our office first borrowed winter grain from various counties, and then borrowed cash from banks. We even moved and appropriated slaughter tax deposits, almost exhausting our resources. We have previously written to your committee, requesting you to quickly convene a meeting to discuss relief methods and open up new taxes, so that our office can have something to follow. Currently, the funds for the various schools for September and October have been decided by the Audit Committee. Funds for September have been allocated to the counties, and funds for half a month have been allocated for October. There are few reserves in the current treasury, and we must also raise funds for the winter study abroad expenses for various countries. Beyond this, we will have nothing to borrow and nothing to raise. Even when the counties have a prosperous harvest season, the grain tax has already been spent in advance. The schools require monthly expenses that cannot be intermittent. At this critical moment, we are on the verge of bankruptcy. If we do not quickly find a way to provide relief, how can we face the education of the entire province and look forward to the future without feeling terrified? Your committee is responsible for coordinating the education funds of the entire province, so how can you bear to sit idly by? Our office is responsible for management, so how dare we remain silent? Therefore, we are compelled to bother you again and again, and present to you in detail the situation of the shortfall in income and expenses for this year. According to the budget of 4,896,552 yuan for this year, our office estimates the revenue from various taxes to be 3,700,000 yuan, assuming the most prosperous harvest year. Currently, from the beginning of the year, July 1st to November 15th, the revenue from various taxes is 815,324.34 yuan, the amount borrowed from the grain tax is 313,273.36 yuan, and the amount borrowed from the bank is 120,000 yuan, totaling 1,248,597.7 yuan. Furthermore, 339,837.62 yuan has been allocated to the counties for school expenses, and 71,337.7 yuan in expenses have been issued but not transferred from the previous year, totaling 1,659,772.39 yuan. It is estimated that by the end of the year, in addition to the borrowed and allocated funds mentioned above, we can still collect 2,040,227.61 yuan from various taxes, plus 171,980 yuan in school administrative revenue, totaling 2,212,270.61 yuan. On the expenditure side, in addition to the surplus of 90,528.37 yuan from the previous year, 410,101.27 yuan has been taken from this year's revenue, and 1,233,504.35 yuan in expenses have already been spent in the first half of the year from July to October. According to the full-year budget, we still need 3,660,347.65 yuan to balance the budget by next June. This leaves a shortfall of 1,458,840.4 yuan. Adding the 135,000 yuan borrowed from the slaughter tax deposit from the previous year, the total shortfall is 1,585,840.4 yuan. Even if the subsidies from the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Finance listed in the budget are received in full, it will still be insufficient, and there is no certainty of that. The numbers listed above are all based on actual calculations, and cannot be glossed over with empty words. We urge your committee to investigate the previous cases, quickly convene an emergency meeting to discuss relief measures, and we are extremely anxious to await your orders. Furthermore, the Provincial Department of Finance subsidizes 300,000 yuan, and the Provincial Government decided to allocate 25,000 yuan per month, but so far only 10,000 yuan has been received for July. Also, an order to pay 15,000 yuan has been repeatedly negotiated with the bank, but has not yet been received. As for the other months, we have repeatedly requested in vain. As for the 200,000 yuan from the Ministry of Finance, our office has no basis for it. We are attaching this information for your reference. This is to the Jiangsu Education Funds Committee.

Ministry of Education Holds Review Meeting for Agricultural Courses in Senior High Schools

Yesterday morning, the Ministry of Education held a review meeting for the curriculum standards for agricultural courses in senior high schools. Chen Zongyi, Fu Huangguang, Gu Shusen, and others attended. The results of the detailed review of the draft standards for each subject revealed the following three shortcomings in the draft standards: (1) the standards are too high, (2) the level of each subject is not consistent with the opinions of the experts, and (3) the curriculum lacks flexibility. They should be submitted for review. Sun Yushu and Wang Qihua are requested to review the general agriculture curriculum. Wang Qihua is requested to review the sericulture course. Fu Huangguang and Chen Zongyi are requested to review the forestry course. After the review is completed, another meeting will be held to discuss them.

Jiangwan and Zhenru Win West Youth Basketball Games Last Night

26 to 23

40 to 34

Last night, the West Youth Basketball Association held a total of three games. The results were: (1) Eagle Team defeated Jiyong (Group B), 26 to 23; (2) Jiangwan defeated Zhonggong (Group A), 31 to 21; (3) Zhenru defeated Huadong (Group A), 40 to 34. The last game was the most intense and exciting.

(1) Eagle Team Wins Jiyong (B1)

This was a Group B game. The strength of the two teams was very close, and the competition was very fierce. Jiyong was one of Guanghua's teams. The situation was very good in the first half, winning 12 to 10. Unfortunately, the Eagle Team caught up quickly in the second half, and the Eagle Team won 26 to 23. Hu Zhikang, the left forward of the Eagle Team, scored 14 points alone.

(2) Jiangwan Defeats Zhonggong (Group A)

Jiangwan shows its power this time Jiangwan (Fudan athletes) has a very strong strength, and it seems easy to defeat Zhonggong yesterday, and Zhonggong's failure to throw the basket may also be due to bad luck. At first, Zhang Jinxiang from Jiangwan opened the scoring, and Guan Yi from Zhonggong returned it. Mo Mingquan, the center of Jiangwan, raised his hand for a long shot and took the lead. Mo and Wu Shuqian continued to make contributions, but Zhonggong was unable to do anything. The first half was 13 to 6, and Jiangwan won.

Zhonggong's setback Zhonggong's defenders seem to be stronger than the forwards, but defending against Fudan's three forwards is very difficult. Mo Mingquan is a famous player with a majestic demeanor, scoring one after another with lively and agile skills. There is no comparison at one time. Zhonggong was badly hurt in the first half, and although He Yanzhang succeeded in a long shot, it was quite difficult to recover. Jiangwan finally defeated it by 31 to 21.

Smooth sailing Zhenru is also a strong team, and it is difficult to say who is better than Huadong. Sneak attack successfully In the second half, Huadong's momentum suddenly increased. Liang Guoquan scored nine points in a row with his exquisite skills, resulting in a 25-point tie. The whole game suddenly became tense. Lu Zhongen succeeded in a sneak attack under the basket and suddenly took the lead with 27 to 25.

Long shots repeatedly made The victory of Zhenru over Huadong can be said to be due to the accuracy of their shooting. Huang Li can be called a pair of heroes, and their repeated long shots are the fatal injury of Huadong. After the score was tied at 30-30, Zhenru repeatedly shot and made, and finally won 40-34. The referee was Belle Si.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Sea Guest

Father—Child, you've already eaten three bowls of rice today. Your stomach must be full. Why do you want to add more?

Son—I still don't feel full. Besides, the dishes are so good today.

Father—You're so greedy. If people see you, they might say you're a little pig. Do you know what a little pig is?

Son—I know. A little pig is the son of an old pig, isn't it?

Doctor (after eating a meal in a restaurant, asks the waiter)—How much is it altogether?

Waiter—Altogether it's one dollar and twenty cents.

Doctor (fumbling around)—Oh dear. I only brought one dollar with me today. What should I do? Ah, I have an idea. Let me take a look at your tongue and check your pulse.

Waiter—What's that supposed to be?

Doctor—I think you might be sick. Consider the twenty cents a special, discounted consultation fee.

Woman A—Mr. C wrote to me this time to propose marriage. His words in the letter were unusually sincere, saying he'd rather die than not marry me. But I returned it to him. He didn't seem to mind. What's the reason for that?

Woman B—Ah. He's originally a novelist. When he submits manuscripts to bookstores, nine out of ten get returned. So, he's used to it.

A Record of the Field Drill in Pudong

— Wang Naixiu

Since Mr. He Yingqin took office as Director-General of Training, he issued an order that students above high school level must receive two years of military training. Our Minli Middle School actively implemented it with outstanding results. Military instructor Liu Fenglin's instruction emphasized strictness and practicality. Therefore, on the 21st of this month, he led the healthy soldiers to the field drill at Yangsi Bridge in Pudong, and specially purchased fifty dollars of firecrackers to use as imitation bullets. On that day, the sky was high and clear, and the wind was gentle and sunny. At 8 a.m., the three companies of healthy soldiers were lined up on the field, full of energy. The first company was fully armed with rifles. The second and third companies carried water bottles and food bags, etc. The bags contained bread and fruit for lunch. Under the fluttering flags and the sound of military music, instructor Liu led the departure. The military band marched at the head of the line, and the military appearance along the way was solemn and the pace was neat, which was awe-inspiring. When we arrived at the Gaochangmiao riverside pier, we bought seven boats to cross the river. Swaying in the heart of the river, we could see the scenery on both sides at a glance. The sound of the water was gurgling, and the sound of the wind rustling responded to each other. Warships and wheel boats were parked in a row along the coast. The Yixian ship, which was launched on the birthday of the President, was also berthed here. From a distance, the ship was freshly painted and very majestic. Before long, we arrived at Zhoujiadu in Pudong. We disembarked and proceeded to Yangsi Bridge. After walking for two li, instructor Liu ordered the first platoon of the first company to be the vanguard, advancing alone to scout whether there were enemy ambushes ahead, and sent two sentries to stand guard on the mounds. The rear teams divided up the firecrackers and prepared for the field battle. Each class had a bugler to signal. When the vanguard soldiers waved the lure flag, the sentries would rush back to report the discovery of the enemy. Instructor Liu then directed the platoon leaders to lead their subordinates to disperse and skirmish on the tombs on both sides of the railway. The soldiers of each class were ambushed in the rear, lit the firecrackers and began shooting. For a time, the sound of explosions was like thunder, and the smoke filled the air as if they were in a rain of bullets. Suddenly, the sound of a march was heard, and the soldiers of each class also echoed the drums. Our army crouched and held guns, bravely charging forward, killing sounds were shaking the sky, like rabbits escaping. After about hundreds of paces, they still chose a place to hide and continue shooting for about twenty minutes. When the return signal sounded loudly, they lowered their flags and silenced their drums, returned to the team, and assembled. Everyone was covered in mud. The drill was over. They went straight to Yangsi Primary School in Yangsi Bridge to rest. Each took out the bread they carried for lunch. After a short rest, they lined up and called the roll. Instructor Liu gave a speech, commending them for their hard work. On the way back, they were still full of energy and without any fatigue. By the time they returned to school, the sun had already set.

Various Kinds of Crabs

— Yang Yixiao

The taste of crab is the freshest, so everyone likes to eat it. In addition to fresh cooking, there are also methods such as quick marinating, drunken marinating, and paste marinating. Crab lovers should know how to choose.

Quick-Marinated Crab: Take the crab, wash it, and put it in a jar. Add scallions, ginger, and good soy sauce, and seal it tightly for three days. After the soy sauce has penetrated, it can be opened and eaten.

Drunken Crab: First put the crab in a jar and pour in two catties of old wine. Seal it tightly. The so-called jade marrow and golden paste are deeply brewed.

Paste Crab: Use live crabs, fermented rice wine, and fresh paste. The paste and meat are tender and delicious, like fresh paste eggs. It should be eaten within two or three days after opening.

Soybean Paste Crab: Choose small round-navel crabs. Put them in a jar and steam them over water until cooked. After taking them out, spread the shells with soybean paste and put them in a large bowl and mix well. It can be eaten in three days.

Anecdotes from a Solo Exhibition

— Yu Jianhua

This untalented individual, in recent years, due to family upheavals and environmental pressures, having no one to confide in about all the suffering, grief, and indignation, has poured it all into painting. This has slightly alleviated the pent-up resentment, and my painting has also made some progress as a result. However, the sea of art is vast, and a vole can only drink so much. How much can I achieve? With my meager understanding, I earnestly wish to seek guidance from those who are knowledgeable, so I am publicly exhibiting nearly a hundred recent works and have specially arranged a preview, respectfully inviting renowned artists in Shanghai to offer their corrections, so that I may follow them. I have been wrongly showered with praise, excessively adorned, and people have competed to order my works, which were instantly sold out. This has resulted in those who came to the opening unable to satisfy their viewing desires. I had no choice but to hold a second exhibition for pre-orders, to avoid disappointment. Unexpectedly, in less than two days, pre-orders exceeded a hundred pieces. The date for the second opening was set for the twentieth and twenty-first days of the twelfth lunar month, which is very soon. I dare not be greedy for more and act hastily, disappointing those with refined tastes. Therefore, I stopped pre-orders ahead of schedule. Those who wished to pre-order on the third day had to wait until next year, and yet, another sixty or so pieces were pre-ordered in a single day. I have always been known among my peers for the speed of my production, but even I am now exhausted from keeping up. It is estimated that in the three days of the exhibition, in addition to the hundred exhibited pieces being completely sold out, more than a hundred and seventy pieces were pre-ordered. And the number of visitors reached more than three thousand. Even senior masters like Cheng Yaosheng graced us with their presence, breaking protocol. I am deeply concerned that my talent is limited, my knowledge is shallow, my brush is clumsy, and my ink is inferior, and that I will not be able to meet the earnest expectations of all circles. I can only strive to improve myself and dare not be complacent about this. Among the exhibited works, No. 33, "Southern Mountain Green Screen," and No. 86, "Autumn River Evening Ferry," received the most pre-orders. On the first day, fourteen people each ordered them. On the second day, No. 33 increased to eighteen people, and No. 86 increased to twenty-four people. On the third day, No. 33 increased to twenty-nine people, and No. 86 actually increased to forty-five people. Red stickers were lined up in two rows from the axis to the top, with no room to spare. A friend jokingly said that the two paintings were quite like the "Grand Champion" in horse racing. A Japanese person, Yamada Kenkichi, ordered one of No. 33, and a German person, Fang Haler, ordered one of No. 86, also distantly facing each other. Next were No. 65, "Reading the Yi in a Pine Studio," with nineteen people, and No. 1, "Three Peaks on the River," with ten people. And the original orderers of these four paintings were Zhang Shanzi, Zhang Daqian, and Huang Binhong, the president of the painting society, two brothers, and one person, all living in the same house, which is quite remarkable. The discerning eyes of famous artists are indeed extraordinary. On the morning of the second day, as soon as the arrangement was completed, only two or three visitors came, and the album of pages, "Serving Mother," which was not for sale, had mysteriously disappeared. A thorough search yielded nothing. On the third day, a friend came from an antique tea party and said, "Yesterday, someone was selling an album of pages, asking for a loan of two hundred yuan." This gentleman's technique of opening boxes does not concede to the legendary thief "Amazing Hands Empty." It is a pity that my paintings are not worth much money; it is a bit of a waste of a great talent.

Mei Lanfang's Upcoming Performance

— Master of the Vase Studio

Changing strategy to perform more old plays

After returning north from performing last year, Mei Lanfang declared that he would no longer appear on stage. The connoisseurs of Shanghai, upon hearing this news, were all disappointed. Now, good news has arrived: Mei Lanfang will come to Shanghai to sing again, to bid a final farewell to the people of Shanghai. Therefore, this performance by Mei Lanfang is even more worthy of our excitement. It is said that Mei Lanfang plans to change his strategy this time, performing more old plays and fewer new ones. Such as "The Mad Woman" (Cosmic Rhyme), the complete version, "Snow Cup Edge," "Yu Tang Chun," "Woman Escorted," "Four Lang Visits His Mother," "Farewell My Concubine," "Sacrificing to the River," "Thirteen Sisters," "The Drunken Concubine," and other plays, will be performed in order to meet the needs of all circles. (The Beka Company has the films of Mei's "Visiting Mother," "Cosmic Rhyme," "Woman Escorted," and "Farewell to Tang Dynasty," and sales are surprisingly strong. This proves the popularity of old plays in the musical theater world.) As for the full-length play "Yang Guifei," which he arranged himself, the subject matter is righteous and the arrangement is appropriate. In the areas of Tianjin and Peking, every performance is sold out. Its charm is not weaker than that of the old plays. Therefore, he also plans to perform it this time, so that those who love to watch new plays will not have the regret of missing out. (Mei's three "Yang Guifei" recordings at Beka, with dialogue and singing, are extremely well-structured. The "Erh Huang Duoban" melody is novel and is one of the most brilliant parts of the complete "Yang Guifei.")

Record of Dismissing a Concubine

— Yan Ye

There is a Mr. Zhang, a guest in Shanghai. In a certain year, he once held a military command, and after much hard work, he was able to write proclamations. He was especially skilled in poetry and had the reputation of being a refined general. Now that he has resigned, he enjoys poetry and wine all the more. His later years are extremely joyful. Zhang has two concubines, who are sisters, who were bought from a brothel by his friend and presented to him many years ago. They are deeply favored by Zhang, burning incense and adding tea, never leaving his side. When he goes out, he also takes them with him. In the beautiful days of spring and autumn, in the famous scenic areas of Suzhou and Zhejiang, there are often traces of them. They look like celestial couples. This autumn, Zhang took his two concubines to the West Lake again, staying at his friend's house. In a few days, they had traveled all over the North and South Peaks. One day, they went to Lingyin Temple. After touring around, as they were about to leave, a monk suddenly stepped forward, put his palms together, and said, "Sir, are you enjoying your tour of West Lake? Traveling by the lake, with women in the carriage, leisurely on the water, carrying the West Lake with you, you are truly like a celestial being." Zhang was stunned. He stared at him for a long time, as if he recognized him. He said, "Are you so-and-so? Why are you a monk now?" The monk said, "Yes. I was your commander in a certain regiment under you. I have been here for three years." When asked why he entered the monastery, he smiled and said nothing. He only asked about Zhang's residence. Zhang returned to his residence, feeling disappointed. He stayed indoors for three days. Suddenly, a messenger came, delivering a letter to Zhang. He opened it and saw a few words. After reading it, he slammed the table in anger, then became silent, and finally shed tears. He then threw the letter into the fire. He hastily led his two concubines back to Shanghai. People were very surprised. After Zhang returned to Shanghai, he went out at night and did not return. When he returned the next morning, he took out two thousand gold coins from his pocket and placed them in front of the two women, ordering each to take half, saying, "Now we part. Take this with you and return to your hometown. Having this, you can live in the countryside for the rest of your life. The world is colorful, but it is useless to linger. Brothels are even more of a hell. Do not fall into it again." The two women did not want to leave, and tears fell like rain. Zhang had no pity and urged them to leave quickly. The two women knew they could not stay, so they each took their belongings and left crying. As they reached the door, they still turned their heads. Zhang smiled and waved them goodbye, repeatedly shouting, "Relief! Relief!" After the two women left, Zhang spent all day writing in the air, grumbling to himself. Ten days later, he left his family and has been gone for two months. No one knows where he is. I heard about this and said it was a strange thing. So I recorded it.

Travelogue to Southeast Asia (85)

— Ling Hua

July 2nd, rain. Wanted to visit the zoo, but couldn't understand the local language and returned without finding it. Mr. Yang Jiangshui came and offered to take me. So I went with him. Exited 22nd Chinatown, went on White Pagoda Road. The tram costs two copper coins per person. The trams in Rangoon are not as crowded as those in Japan and Shanghai. The ticket seller is also experienced and treats customers calmly. The level of our Chinese citizens is not even as good as that of Siam, and still below that of the Burmese. If you don't believe it, try comparing it with the tram drivers. Passed the Buddhist boys' school established by Queen Victoria of England. There is also a Buddhist girls' school established by Queen Victoria. Is this also a way to appease the Burmese? Got off the tram at the Great Golden Pagoda. Then took a small horse-drawn carriage. Three annas for two people, a total of twelve copper coins. Then arrived at the zoo. The road is very clean. Forests and lakes surround the park. But I had no guide at first. Couldn't find my way around a small area. A car asked for two shields from me. Each shield is worth one yuan and three cents in Chinese currency. Alas. The wonderful realm of the Great Dao is right in front of us. With a guide, it is easy to find. Without a guide, one is lost. From this, we can understand that the world cannot be without a great teacher. The entrance ticket is two annas, each anna being four copper coins. This park is a famous park in East Asia. The scale is quite impressive. The architecture has different points. It is very different from the Beijing Zoo. Although the latter has a large number of animals and plants, the architecture and management of this place are worth learning from. I hope that future visitors will pay attention to it. Because it is not easy to keep animals in a zoo, the technology of feeding, management, and architecture needs to be studied. But although its location is large, there are not many types of animals.

Upon entering the park, I first saw several lions, grayish-blue in color. The sizes of the males and females were also roughly equal. Next were several tigers. People say that there is the character "king" on the tiger's head. It's true. All the houses here have a space below to avoid moisture. The tiger sheds are also like this, living on the floor. The excrement must be swept and washed by workers. When workers want to enter the tiger's shed, they first use iron rods to trick the tigers into the inner room. After the tigers enter, the iron gate in the room suddenly falls from above. The workers can then enter and sweep the excrement. But this method is quite clumsy. It seems that a better method needs to be devised.

Warmth in My Heart (323)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Diligently Asks the Teacher for Writing Advice; Generously Discussing Military Affairs, the Heroine Parties in a Brothel

Most of those who make a living through writing suffer from stomach problems. And eating that kind of packed lunch makes people even more uncomfortable. If you come out after having dinner at home, the time isn't right. Going back late means you'll be hungry. Although there are occasional social gatherings, or someone invites the reporters from the newspaper to have dinner, this is a particularly rare occurrence. Because in the past, society in general didn't value the press as much as it does now. People in political circles regarded them as the scum of intellectuals. Ordinary people also said that they were just talking nonsense, and didn't know that newspapers were a propaganda machine. Inviting a reporter to dinner has little effect. And the reporters of the past were unwilling to eat other people's food easily, as if eating their food would shut their mouths. There had to be an introduction and a clear understanding of the facts. They wouldn't just come when beckoned and leave when dismissed. They had to maintain a certain aloofness, a bit of an arrogant attitude, unlike the approachability they have now. There were even two reporters who absolutely wouldn't attend outside social functions, preferring to burn a kerosene stove and eat rice soaked in tea in their small rooms, unwilling to parade around in the name of a reporter. Therefore, when it came to the dinner problem, it was best to have two or three close friends, drink wine, and talk. Fortunately, there are many restaurants in Shanghai. Eating at this one tonight, and that one tomorrow. It doesn't cost much, and you can change the flavor every night. This can be considered a joy among friends. It's just that these consecutive nights of dinners for Zuo Shichen all involved meeting with Green Intent. Once people become familiar, all shyness disappears. Before, when a lady came to sing, she would always sit quietly to the side, looking down and fiddling with her handkerchief. If you looked at her, she would smile back at you. If you asked her a question, she would at most answer you with one sentence. Sometimes that one sentence would be shortened to two words, one word. If you asked further, there would be no words at all. Or she would nod or shake her head to indicate her agreement or disagreement. It took five or six nights, like a connoisseur playing with an antique jade, gradually getting familiar. On stage, she would gradually talk and laugh. Plus, there was Ah Su by her side, like a musician accompanying. Because Green Intent had a shortcoming: she couldn't sing very well. Although she could hum a few lines, she thought she sang poorly and was afraid to sing. This suited Zuo Shichen's temperament. Zuo Shichen said, "I just don't understand singing. If I don't understand, I don't understand. Why pretend to be an expert?" Sometimes, if someone who was good at singing came along, they could sing with proper rhythm and inflection, and everyone would clap in time, which was naturally very good. The listeners would find it enjoyable, and the singer would add to the excitement. But if someone who wasn't very good at singing was forced to sing, they would turn red in the face and neck, exhaust themselves, and the song they sang would still be a bit out of tune. It's better to hide your clumsiness.
