Stock Exchange Revises Settlement Date for Next Month

And Announces Settlement Date for January of Year 20

The futures settlement period for the Securities Exchange's December of Year 19 was originally scheduled for December 30th. However, due to accounting considerations among brokers, a special request was made to the Exchange to advance the settlement. The Exchange's Board of Directors has resolved to move the December futures settlement forward to December 29th. At the same time, it was also decided to suspend market trading from the 30th of this month and reopen the market on January 5th of Year 20. In addition, the January futures settlement for Year 20 has also been determined by the Exchange's Board of Directors to be on January 30th. An announcement has been issued in the Exchange's market. The two announcements are recorded below:

(1) Having received a letter from the Brokers Association requesting that the settlement date for December, as stipulated by the Exchange, be moved forward due to accounting considerations, the Exchange's Board of Directors has resolved that all December futures settlements, originally scheduled for the 30th, will now be changed to the 29th. Furthermore, the market will be closed for vacation from the 30th, and the market will reopen as usual on January 5th of the Republic of China Year 20.

(2) The Exchange's Board of Directors resolved yesterday to set January 30th of the Republic of China Year 20 as the date for January futures settlement.

Local News

Banking Community's Announcement Regarding the Reorganization of Domestic Debt Yesterday

Representatives of the Tianjin banking community have been determined.

A creditor group can be established within ten days.

The Shanghai, Beijing, and Tianjin banking communities initiated the organization of a Chinese domestic debt creditor group to register group accounts and request reorganization. According to yesterday's news, in addition to the representatives of the Shanghai and Beiping banking communities' creditor groups, the Tianjin banking community also telegraphed back to the local banking association yesterday, saying that Sun Zhongshan, the manager of Tianjin Dazhong Bank, Ding Wenchao, the manager of Huiye Bank, and Zhu Yusheng, the manager of Yanye Bank, have been determined as representatives, and they will leave for Shanghai immediately to participate. The representatives of Beijing and Tianjin are expected to arrive in Shanghai within a week. After the representatives of Beijing and Tianjin arrive in Shanghai, the representatives in Shanghai will first have an informal agreement, and then officially meet to establish a creditor group of the banking sector. Matters such as the registration and detailed investigation of creditors nationwide, the names and amount statistics of various new and old domestic debts, and the reorganization plan will also be discussed at this meeting. Because the majority of the debt amount of the national new and old domestic debts is owed, the creditor group must be initiated first to obtain a thorough reorganization.

Leftover News from the Support Xiao and Anti-Dutch Conference

The Diplomatic Support Association will convene soon.

The situation of the public support Xiao and anti-Dutch conference held by all sectors at the City Chamber of Commerce the day before yesterday has been recorded in yesterday's newspaper, but because the meeting was adjourned too late, the details of the meeting were not covered by various newspapers, so the leftover news is added as follows.

Worker donations. At the end of the meeting, Chairman Xu Jigong reported to the public that the Greater China Record Company donated 100 yuan for the conference and the Diplomatic Support Association. The crowd applauded greatly. It is heard that the company was founded by overseas Chinese, so its workers are particularly familiar.

The representative is determined to petition. The representative, Xu Jigong and other five people, were publicly recommended by the public, and it was agreed to set off that night to rush to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to urge the issuance of electricity to the Dutch side as soon as possible to abolish the unequal "Sino-Dutch Consular Treaty" and negotiate the correction of the unequal regulations in the Dutch Charter that "Chinese are assimilated to the natives" and cancel the Dutch Parliament's resolution on increasing the entry tax for overseas Chinese to 150 guilders per person and the pier tax for continued residence of Chinese workers to 75 guilders per person. If the goal is not achieved, they will not leave the Ministry.

The Support Association. The name and brief of this association have been discussed for a long time. Finally, it was decided that all the 21 groups that initiated the convocation, such as the Overseas Chinese Federation, would be ex officio members, and all the groups that attended the meeting that day would join the organization, and the Overseas Chinese Federation would be publicly recommended to convene the first meeting.

Continue to send telegrams. (1) "Telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, please seriously negotiate the case according to the main points decided by the conference, and ask to replace the stubborn and shameless Consul General Zhang." The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Jun Jian, our country's female teacher Xiao Xin'an was brutally raped by the Dutch second mate of the Zhawagongsi轮船芝巴德号 in turn. Anyone with blood could not help but feel indignant. Therefore, on the 26th of this month, all sectors of Shanghai were convened at the Chamber of Commerce in this city to publicly support Xiao and oppose the Dutch conference. More than 100 groups and thousands of representatives arrived and immediately discussed and decided on several minimum requirements for the Xiao case, (1) The Dutch government must formally apologize to our government and guarantee that the same facts will never happen again in the future, (2) Zhawagongsi must publish in all Chinese and Western newspapers in all places where overseas Chinese reside, apologize to our entire nation and Ms. Xiao, and guarantee that the same facts will never happen again in the future, (3) Severely punish the Dutch first mate Lan Anqi and the second mate Lei Dima Kai, who took turns raping on the Zhawagongsi轮船芝巴德号, and must not only be dismissed or demoted, (4) Permanently remove the shipowner of the Zhawagongsi输船亚尔氏 and the ship doctor 白林古, who were in the same evil, and must not only be demoted, (5) Zhawagongsi will compensate Ms. Xiao Xin'an for the loss of 100,000 taels. We sincerely request that the Ministry obey public opinion and seriously negotiate. If the Dutch side does not accommodate, our country's boycott of Dutch ships and all anti-Dutch movements will never stop. Recently, I heard that Consul General Zhang in Java telegraphed the Ministry, saying that the Zhawagongsi in Batavia claimed that the first mate and second mate had been demoted and were being tried by the court, and asked the Xiamen and Shanghai municipal governments to stop the boycott, etc. If the Consul General really had this telegram, he was insane. Whether Ms. Xiao is a member of our nation, despising and raping Ms. Xiao is equivalent to despising and raping our entire nation. Even if the Consul General privately and forcibly expelled Ms. Xiao from the Chinese nation, even if only a personal rape lawsuit would never be settled by demotion. May I ask Consul General Zhang, if overseas Chinese rape Dutch women, can the Consul General guarantee that overseas Chinese will not be subject to other penalties besides being demoted? As for the court trial, it is only a perfunctory means. There is absolutely no value for consideration before the sentence is imposed. The Consul General dared to speak for the enemy without arguing according to reason. Please ask the Ministry to immediately remove the Consul General to show the determination to love the country and overseas Chinese and to warn the stubborn and shameless people. A telegram of grief and indignation is sent, and the clear order is expected. The Support Xiao and Anti-Dutch Conference of all sectors in Shanghai bows down. (2) "Telegram to the Fujian Provincial Government, please stop the Xiamen authorities (banning the boycott of Zhawa ships) from issuing chaotic orders." The Fujian Provincial Government, Jun Jian, our country's female teacher Xiao Xin'an was brutally raped by the Dutch second mate of the Zhawagongsi轮船芝巴德号, and the whole world was indignant. In addition, the Dutch government has massacred tens of thousands of our compatriots over the years, imprisoned and expelled countless party reporters and teachers, and levied tens of millions of yuan in head tax and wartime income tax on our people. In its governing Dutch charter, it publicly stipulates that Chinese people are an inferior nation and are in the same category as the natives, which is even more unbearable. Therefore, the whole country has risen up and unanimously boycotted Zhawa ships as a diplomatic backing. The Xiamen Support Xiao Case Committee has organized a patrol team to boycott Dutch ships, which is enough to represent the public opinion of the whole body. The general manager of Zhawagongsi in Shanghai, at the beginning of advocating the boycott in our port, immediately sent a representative, Qian Chongfu, to apologize to the Overseas Chinese Federation, willing to publish in the name of Zhawagongsi in Chinese and Western newspapers in all places where overseas Chinese reside, apologize to the entire Chinese nation and Ms. Xiao, and guarantee that the same facts will never happen again in the future. American Overseas Celebrates Thanksgiving Day Yesterday

Pray and have a feast

Yesterday was the American Thanksgiving Day, which is to celebrate the harvest and thank God for the abundance of the five grains, just like the ancient Chinese La sacrifice. Since 1621, the United States has stipulated it as a law and has been following it every year. Every year in late November, the President chooses a Thursday to hold it, and prepares a prayer text to be promulgated throughout the country. At that time, the officials will read it respectfully to show their piety. The American overseas and soldiers and students in this port also gathered at the Grand Chapel of Sanma Road at 11:00 a.m. to make a grand prayer. The American Consul General, Qin Jintu, read the President's blessing. In the evening, every family held a celebration banquet, and the Marine Corps and warships were also given a day off to set up a feast. Items such as turkey and American fruits were essential items on the table that day.

Chen Mingshu Meets with Representatives of the Industrial Association

Zhong Lingjun, a student studying in France, usually pays attention to craftsmanship and has no contact with comrades in France. In order to avoid losing the research, the Republic of China

Photograph of Chen Mingshu Receiving Representatives from the French Industrial Society

From right to left: Mr. Zhong Ling, inventor of the Zhong Ling Printing Machine; Mr. Xu Kuangwu, inventor of artificial ivory; Ms. Zhong Duqing, female calligrapher; Mr. Chen Mingshu, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government; Miss Ouyang, daughter of the Guangzhou Public Security Bureau Chief; Mr. Gao Muhong, mechanical engineer who studied in France.

(Photo by this newspaper)

In the fourteenth year (of the Republic, i.e., 1925), the Society of Arts and Crafts Research was established in Paris. At that time, Gao Muhong, Xu Kuangwu, Zhong Yu, and others jointly organized dozens of Chinese students studying arts and crafts in France to join, researching together as a group. After returning to China, they dispersed to various places, maintaining infrequent communication. Zhong Ling and others believed that it was necessary to establish the Society in Shanghai. In October of this year, they sent circulars to former members, convening a general meeting at No. 44 Huang Lu Road, dedicated to studying the needs of Chinese industry and encouraging each other. On the 27th of this month, Chairman Chen Mingshu of the Guangdong Provincial Government arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing. The Society members, having always admired Chairman Chen's respect for industry, sent representatives Zhong Nan, Gao Muhong, Xu Kuangwu, and Zhong Yu to pay their respects and offer many contributions regarding the future of Chinese industry. Chairman Chen expressed great sympathy for the Society representatives and promised appropriate assistance in the future. The representatives were overjoyed and requested a group photograph to commemorate the occasion.

Mr. Ohtani Flew to Nanjing Yesterday

Four Organizations Scheduled a Banquet

Mr. Raizo Ohtani, head of Da Lai (Ohtani Kisen Co.), came to Shanghai from the United States this time to develop Far East shipping and to inaugurate new routes to the inner parts of Luzon, and he attended the inaugural ceremony. He once told people that Pacific shipping this year has reached a situation of too many ships and not enough cargo, resulting in overcapacity. The shipment of goods from China to the United States is particularly sluggish. Ohtani Kisen has a total of seventeen ships traveling between China and the United States. In this period of shipping decline, it is necessary to find ways to remedy the situation. In addition to the two giant ships being built for the Sino-American line, which will be launched next month and in January of next year, there are currently few excellent passenger ships sailing in the inner parts of Luzon. The company has specially built a new passenger ship at a cost of 4 million pesos, dedicated to operating between the islands of Manila. It was launched this month and will be sufficient in future business to compensate for the inadequacy of the Sino-American line. The war in China has ended, and construction is just beginning. In the future, trade between the two countries will surely flourish, and Sino-American shipping will soon be able to recover. After returning to Shanghai from Luzon via Guangzhou, Mr. Ohtani felt slightly unwell due to exposure to the elements, but he recovered yesterday. Since he must return to the United States via the Pacific next week, he took advantage of his remaining free time to go to the capital. This trip is to meet with important officials of the National Government. He originally planned to go to Nanjing by train, but because it would take longer, he went to Hongqiao Airport yesterday morning with Mr. Steding, the Shanghai manager, and Secretary Gibson, and flew to Nanjing together. He will visit President Chiang Kai-shek and will have to return to Shanghai in about one or two days.

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Banking Association, the Money Trade Association, and the Shipping Association have specifically scheduled a banquet for Mr. Ohtani on the second of next month to strengthen their friendship. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has already sent out invitations, inviting leaders of the city's industry and commerce to attend.

Various Organizations Prepare to Welcome British Economic Mission

The Riri News reports that the British Economic Mission led by Thomson and others will come to China, as has been reported in various newspapers. The various organizations in Shanghai believe that the arrival of this mission is of great importance to China's economy. Yesterday, the Bureau of Social Affairs, the Diplomatic Office in Shanghai, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau jointly organized a preparatory welcome committee. They met at the Jianghai Customs Building to discuss all welcome preparations. Those present included Tian Heqing, representative of the Bureau of Social Affairs; Ye Muqiao, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Guan Chengqing, representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; and Huang Dingxun, representative of the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau. The following resolutions were made: (1) Each organization will send personnel to the dock on the 30th of this month to welcome the mission; (2) Guides will be assigned to lead the mission on tours of various places; (3) The mission will be accompanied to Nanjing by the British Chamber of Commerce on Wednesday next week (December 3); (4) All organizations are notified that if they wish to host a welcome banquet, they must notify the Bureau of Social Affairs in advance to schedule the date and order. The dates for visiting various places in Shanghai are scheduled as follows: "December 1, visit the piece goods and cotton textile companies on Hong Kong Road in the morning; December 2, visit the Zhen Tai Textile Company in the morning, discuss the visiting schedule at the British Chamber of Commerce in the afternoon, and then visit the yarn and woolen textile companies; December 3, go to Nanjing; December 6, return to Shanghai by train in the evening; December 8, the British Chamber of Commerce hosts a banquet in the evening; December 10, the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau and the Diplomatic Office host a tea party at 4 pm; December 11, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce hosts a banquet; December 13, the British Chamber hosts a banquet; December 20, go to Beiping." The mission is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 30th of this month aboard the British ship Rawalpindi. Upon arrival, Mr. Barnett, the Commercial Counselor of the British Embassy, will notify the welcome preparation committee to go to the dock to welcome them. After landing, they will stay at the Cathay Hotel. The mission consists of a total of eighteen people, divided into four groups: (1) Commercial Investigation Group, (2) Production Investigation Group, (3) Woolen Textile Investigation Group, (4) Machine Investigation Group. The head of the mission is Mr. Thomson, the General Secretary is Mr. Quinton Hill, the Deputy Secretary is Mr. Barnes, and the Secretary of the Cotton Industry Group is Mr. Cartway.

Process of Allocating and Handling Public Security Funds in Shanghai County

Magistrate Yan reported at the county administration meeting the other day that the Shanghai County public security funds were cut off by the municipal government in June of last year, leaving no source of income. As of January 15 of this year, salaries were paid by submitting a request to the Department of Finance for appropriation, with the arrears of land tax from the 16th year (of the Republic, i.e., 1927) being the main source, and with the approval of borrowing from each district to cover one month's salaries for each branch bureau. The rest was made up by former Magistrate Lu by exhausting all county taxes. At this point, all resources were exhausted, and there was nothing left to borrow. During the tenure of former Magistrate Leng, he continued to request the Department of Finance to allocate 2,000 yuan, and the Property Management Office borrowed 2,000 yuan from the money shops on behalf of the county. Apart from these, the remaining revenue from house taxes and fines for violating regulations, which had always been reserved for clothing expenses, were all diverted to subsidize the food expenses of the police force. Otherwise, there were only arrears, and large debts were owed to each district for rice and temporary loans. In May of this year, the current magistrate again requested the Department of Finance to allocate 2,000 yuan, which was only enough to temporarily maintain the food expenses of the police force. However, the accumulated arrears of salaries were already more than three months. Considering that the lack of funds would undermine public security and affect all facilities, he was deeply worried and sought a solution. After careful consideration of the situation and reviewing the documents, he repeatedly submitted requests to the provincial and municipal authorities for approval and guidance. On the one hand, he settled the accounts with the municipal government for allocation, and on the other hand, he consulted with the municipal government to allocate the county public security funds first. After repeatedly traveling to the province and city, he explained the situation in detail in person. Finally, in June, the municipal government agreed to allocate half of the funds on a monthly basis. However, the monthly expenditure was still far from sufficient. Therefore, he had to temporarily plan for a reduction in staff and provide reduced salaries to maintain operations. However, the previous accumulated debt of more than ten thousand

Page 14

several thousand yuan remained unsettled. During the staff reduction, the arrears of salaries were even more urgent to be paid. In desperation, he again appealed to the provincial authorities to consider the difficult situation and allocate funds to pay the arrears. Recently, approval was granted to allocate 5,000 yuan, but the fundamental solution still depends on the settlement of accounts between the province and the city. This is a summary of the difficult financial situation of the public security funds over the past year and a half. Now, I will separately explain the main points of planning for the allocation of the 5,000 yuan allocated by the province to pay various arrears and related matters, as follows:

(1) General Overview of Arrears (as of November): (1) Total arrears of salaries and wages for public security from January 16 to the end of June: 11,594.342 yuan. According to the above calculation of five and a half months, the monthly expenditure is 3,921.315 yuan, totaling 21,567.15 yuan. The following has been allocated and paid: The Department of Finance allocated funds in advance, totaling 40 yuan. The Property Management Office borrowed 2,000 yuan on behalf of the county. The Municipal Finance Bureau allocated half of the June funds, totaling 1,960.65 yuan. House taxes from each district from January to June totaled 967.15 yuan. 1,028 yuan was diverted from the fines from February to June. The Finance Bureau overspent by 17.008 yuan. The total amount allocated and paid is 9,972.808 yuan. After deducting the amount already allocated and paid, the remaining arrears are as stated above. (2) Advances: Approximately 1,259.578 yuan. According to the above calculation, 1. Balance of summer clothing: 209.12 yuan; 2. Spring clothing, etc.: 288 yuan; 3. Travel expenses for police cadets: 53.47 yuan; 4. Salaries for the remaining police officers for five days in July: 108.988 yuan; 5. Shortfall after staff reduction until this month: approximately 600 yuan. The total is as stated above (Item 2 has not yet been submitted for approval). Item 5 is an estimated amount reported by the Public Security Bureau. (3) Diverted Fines for Violations: Approximately 2,000 yuan. According to the above, the actual revenue from January to June was 1,028 yuan. The actual revenue from July to November has not yet been fully reported. Based on previous estimates, the total is as stated above. The substantial expenses required for clothing in the autumn and winter seasons will be paid from this fund. (4) 2,000 yuan borrowed on behalf of the county by the Property Management Office. (5) 2,288 yuan borrowed from each district in the previous year to cover the expenses of each branch bureau in October. The total of the above arrears is 17,510.386 yuan. This is an approximate amount obtained from reviewing the case files. There are some discrepancies between the amounts allocated by the Public Security Bureau and the former Finance Bureau, which need to be investigated.

(2) Method of Allocation: Except for the expenses borrowed from each district in the previous year to cover the salaries of each branch bureau in October and the loan borrowed on behalf of the county by the Property Management Office, these will be temporarily postponed because the amount allocated this time is too small. 1,500 yuan will be used for the clothing expenses for the autumn and winter seasons, and 3,500 yuan will be used to pay the arrears. 20% of the advances will be paid, the salary for the remaining police officers for five days will be fully paid, and 20% of the remaining advances will also be paid. The arrears of salaries for the branch bureaus in each county will be paid on average by approximately 30%, detailed as follows: A. Portion for Paying Arrears: Total 3,500 yuan. 1. 20% of the advances to Zhu: 144 yuan; 2. Full payment of salaries for the remaining police officers for five days: 108.988 yuan; 3. 20% of other advances: 230.118 yuan; 4. Total payment of arrears to county branch bureaus: 3,027.894 yuan. It should be further stipulated in the above fourth item: (1) 50% of the Zhu advances should be paid, totaling 1,170 yuan; (2) 50% of the temporary loans from each district should be paid, totaling 279 yuan. The remaining 1,538.894 yuan will be received by the bureau and allocated to the county branch bureaus for the payment of police salaries, prioritizing the most urgent needs. B. Portion for Clothing: Total 1,500 yuan. The above is the return of the fines for violations. Because the amount received this time is not large, it cannot be fully returned. Only the clothing needs are met first as stated above. Regarding the above allocation, it needs to be explained that it is difficult to fully repay the loan borrowed on behalf of the county by the Property Management Office. If it is repaid on a pro rata basis, it is also not feasible, so it is planned to postpone it temporarily. The unpaid rice payments from each district are due to the arrearage of salaries. Therefore, more arrearage payments must be made. On the one hand, the hardships of the merchants are also taken into account, reducing the responsibility of each district to bear the burden. Therefore, 50% is paid. Also, because the loans borrowed by each district in the previous year are difficult to repay at this time, 50% of the remaining temporary loans are also paid. However, the listed amounts are based on the reports from the Public Security Bureau. If there are increases or decreases, the allocation should be made according to these figures to avoid repeated allocations and further difficulties. 3. Key Points of Government Planning and Handling: For the past year and a half, the funds have been stopped by the municipal government, and there has been no source of funds. The situation is critical, and the impact on governance is self-evident. Forced by the circumstances, planning and handling have been extremely difficult. In order to maintain the status quo, the government decided to implement staff reductions as soon as the municipal government agreed to allocate half of the funds first. Although it is inevitable to be constrained and simplified, the aim is to avoid the receipt of funds without actual revenue. All personnel serving in public security can work with peace of mind and prevent the arrears of salaries from increasing. This is one aspect. Although there are many accumulated arrears from the past, the provincial government allocated 5,000 yuan during the provincial treasury's difficult times, which is not a small amount. In the past, there was no source of funds, and even maintaining food expenses was difficult. It was out of the question to clear the accumulated arrears. Although the regular expenses are still insufficient, they have been received on a monthly basis. The province has also allocated funds to pay the arrears, so it is necessary to plan comprehensively and allocate them according to the urgency and importance of each item, bringing it to a conclusion. From now on, unless the provincial and municipal authorities settle the allocation and the municipal government allocates the arrears, it will be difficult to raise a large amount of money again in the short term. Therefore, the procedures that have not been cleared for more than a year should be sorted out at this time to avoid making it more difficult to clear them later and to prevent being disturbed by the arrears of salaries in the future, so that they can focus on their duties. This is another aspect. Even after the staff reduction, there is still a monthly shortfall, which means there are still monthly arrears. Fortunately, it has not been long and the amount is not large. This situation should be rectified immediately by tightening the budget again with the funds allocated by the municipal government and the revenue from house taxes, and by reorganizing the budget. The fines must be deposited into the Finance Bureau on a monthly basis according to the regulations, to be used as temporary and clothing expenses. It is hoped that the budget will be appropriate and orderly, waiting for the municipal funds to be allocated according to regulations before restoring the original situation. This is yet another aspect. In short, the difficulties the government has faced in the past with the public security funding issue, the pain experienced by the public security personnel, the difficulties and burdens on all related parties, and the resulting reduction in the efficiency of public security administration, are all evidenced by many facts. If we do not address this now, we will be derelict in our duties. Therefore, after the preliminary plan has been determined, I am presenting this report with the hope that we can all understand the spirit of this and work together towards it.

Savings of Dredging Bureau Transferred to National Bank

Since the founding of the Republic, the dredging expenses of the Dredging Bureau have been funded by the three percent dredging tax collected by the Customs. In recent years, due to the sharp increase in customs duties, the dredging tax has also become abundant. After deducting expenses, the accumulated savings over the years amount to over one million taels. In the past, these funds were placed in fixed-term and current accounts at banks such as HSBC, Mercantile Bank, and British Bank. Since Director Song Ziliang took office, he has found that the bureau's remaining funds are all deposited in foreign banks, which is a loss of national rights. It is heard that he has proposed at the bureau's administrative meeting that since the bureau is a national river dredging agency, all remaining funds should be deposited in a national bank. It has been resolved that the current account savings have already been transferred to the Central Bank for expenses, and that the remaining fixed-term deposits will be transferred to a national bank as soon as they mature.

Various Public Organizations in Baoshan County Telegraph Request to Be Exempted from Construction Bonds

Jiangsu Province has recently issued construction bonds worth 7 million yuan, with the first tranche of 4 million yuan being issued first. It was previously resolved at the provincial government meeting that each county would be allocated a quota to purchase. Baoshan County's quota is 50,000 yuan. It is now known that the various public organizations in the county believe that the years have been lean and the people's resources are truly insufficient. The Public Funds and Property Management Office and various district offices have jointly telegraphed the provincial authorities, requesting exemption from the allocation. The text of the telegram is recorded below: To Ye, Chairman of the Zhenjiang Provincial Government; Sun, Director of the Department of Construction; Chen, Director of the Department of Finance; and Qiu, Magistrate of this county: It has been reported that Jiangsu Province is issuing construction bonds and Baoshan County has been allocated 50,000 yuan to purchase. This county is barren and the people are poor. The financial resources are exhausted. Since the separation of the city and county, the area has been reduced, making it even more difficult. In addition, the autumn harvest has been poor, and the households have little savings. We have already requested a reduction in taxes and truly have no surplus to purchase the bonds. We humbly request that you consider the special circumstances of this county and exempt it from the allocation to alleviate the people's hardship. We are waiting for your orders with utmost respect. Respectfully, Gu Hongchuan, Director of the Public Funds and Property Management Office of Baoshan County; and Lu Fengpu, Wang Qingtao, Yang Weixiong, Shen Buyin, Yan Guangen, etc., district chiefs of various districts.

Two Railway Bureaus Cancel Rice Subsidies

Previously, due to the soaring rice prices, low-paid employees of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways requested the railway bureaus to provide subsidies to help them. The Ministry of Railways approved that those with a monthly salary of more than 30 yuan would receive a rice subsidy of 1.5 yuan, and those with a monthly salary of less than 50 yuan would receive a rice subsidy of 1 yuan. It is now known that the subsidies have been cancelled because the rice prices have now become more stable and the postal service has already implemented the cancellation. Therefore, the railway bureaus have also issued a notice to all departments on the other day that the rice subsidies will be cancelled from December.

Wusong Camp Area Under the Jurisdiction of the Fortress

Military Affairs Ministry's Instruction to Commander Deng

The Wusong Fortress area has a wide camp area, but due to its long history, it is impossible to ascertain the exact number of land acres. As a result, many of them have been occupied by residents as their own. The Ministry of Military Affairs specially sent Hu Qin from the Camp Property Investigation Office to Wusong for an on-site inspection. The inspection has now been completed, and a total of 417 cases have been found, which will be taken back and leased out by the Wusong Fortress to restore property rights. In addition, the old Prince's Mansion in the fortress area was originally built during the late Qing Dynasty and was prepared as a review station for the princes. It was burned down during the Qi-Lu war, leaving only the empty frame. Also, several old barracks such as the Lion Forest have been more than half collapsed. No one has been assigned to manage them, and they have been taken by nearby vagrants, which is not in line with the intention of preserving public property. The Ministry of Military Affairs has instructed the Wusong Fortress Commander to assign personnel nearby to protect the property and emphasize public property. It has also formulated measures for the leasing of camp properties in the Wusong Fortress and ordered Commander Deng to comply. Commander Deng issued an announcement on the other day and put the measures into effect.

Yangtze River Water Levels Rise and Freight Rates Increase

50% Increase Above Wuhu

50% Increase Above Hankou

Six companies including Shanghai's Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin, China Merchants, and San Peh held a meeting yesterday. Due to the daily decrease in river water levels, making navigation difficult and requiring more fuel, they resolved to increase shallow water freight rates. It was agreed at the time that, except for areas below Wuhu where the river is not yet shallow, other ports such as Jiujiang and Hankou would increase export freight rates by 15% of the original price starting from December 1. It was also decided that ports above Hankou, such as Shashi and Yichang, where the water levels are even shallower, would increase freight rates by 50% starting from the first of the month. Notice has already been given to all customers for implementation on schedule. In addition, the shipping companies in North China have also agreed to increase the export freight rates by 10% across the board starting from December 1.

Japanese Ships Expand Shipping Industry to China

Dalian, Guangzhou and Guangdong Lines: Japanese Dalian Steamship Company has been making steady progress in its shipping business to China in recent years. It has added three ships, Fengtian, Changchun, and Dalian, to the Shanghai-Dalian line, and has also opened a special passenger line between Shanghai and Tianjin. In the spring and summer of this year, it built four more cargo ships of 3,500 tons each, namely Kunshan Maru, Qianshan Maru, and Yushan Maru, to operate between Yingkou and Shanghai. Currently, the company is further expanding its operations and has decided to add ships to compete in the Yangtze River shipping industry in China. As for Guangzhou, Xiamen, and Shantou in South China, where the company has no routes, it has also decided to open them at the same time. It will first send two ships to the Yangtze River line and two ships to the Guangzhou line. The company has also commissioned Mitsubishi Shipyard to build four new ships of 4,500 tons each for the development of the Yangtze River and South China shipping business.

Yamashita Expands India-America Line: The Yamashita Company has always had foreign triangular routes, namely those operating to India, North America, and Australia. Recently, due to the sluggish shipping business in the near seas, it has shifted its focus to the ocean. It is heard that it has decided to increase new ships for the India-America lines in the triangular routes in order to compete with various companies for the transportation of timber, cotton, Indian hemp, etc., to the Far East. It is already in the planning stage and will be launched next month.

Kawasaki Opens China-Korea Line: Kawasaki Kisen Co. opened the Yangtze River route and Wenzhou line in Shanghai earlier this year, and then opened the North China route. Now it has added a special China-Korea cargo ship line. Only the Heian Maru of the Chosen Company operates between Shanghai and Korea. Now Kawasaki Kisen Co. has specially assigned the 3,000-ton ship Dongxiang Maru to operate on this route, starting tomorrow. The route will pass through Tianjin, also carrying goods from North China to Korea.

Maiden Voyage Tomorrow

Jardine Matheson's newly built Shanghai-Yichang direct steamer Baohe is now ready after completion of its arrangements. It is scheduled to make its maiden voyage on the 29th of this month, dedicated to the Shanghai-Yichang line. In the future, it will depart from Shanghai on Wednesdays and Saturdays.

Implementation of Stamp Duty Payment for Foreign Insurance Businesses

Promotion Office Invites Chinese Managers to Discuss

Mr. Wang Yanxiang, director of the Stamp Duty Promotion Office for the insurance industry, invited Chinese managers of various foreign companies to attend a discussion on implementation on the other day at the Atlantic Restaurant. Mr. Wang Boqian, the bureau chief's representative, and Mr. Wang Zhaocheng, executive member of the Citizens Federation, attended as guests. Dozens of Chinese managers attended the meeting. First, Director Wang reported on the purpose of the meeting and the process. Then, Mr. Wang Boqian, the representative of the Qian (finance) director, gave a speech, emphasizing that stamp duty is related to the state treasury's revenue and the protection of legal rights. Subsequently, Mr. Wang Zhaocheng and Mr. Li Yongxiang explained the advantages, disadvantages, and obligations. The Chinese managers then discussed the stamp duty payment procedures in a pleasant atmosphere and dispersed.

Northwest Districts' Silk Factory Women Workers Continue to Demand Equal Pay for Men and Women

The Social Affairs Bureau Plans to Convene Mediation Talks

The Eastern District Labor Union Issues a Notice to Comply with Labor-Management Terms

Since the Shanghai Silk Factory strike was mediated by the Social Affairs Bureau, a total of forty-two silk factories have reopened, and most male and female workers are able to work with peace of mind. However, the female workers are dissatisfied with the post-mediation wage cuts, believing that they are not being treated equally with male workers. The female workers of the Eastern District Labor Union took the lead in submitting a petition to the Social Affairs Bureau with certain demands. At that time, the authorities instructed the female workers' representatives to negotiate with the factory management themselves. It is said that the factory management did not agree. Yesterday, the female workers' labor unions in the Northwest districts also submitted the same request to the Social Affairs Bureau. It is said that the Social Affairs Bureau also plans to convene mediation talks at a later date. In other news, the Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Shanghai Eastern District Labor Union Council issued a notice yesterday to its affiliated labor unions regarding the announcement of the Social Affairs Bureau's order No. 4062, which states that the wage reduction dispute in the silk factory industry has been resolved through the Bureau convening representatives from both labor and management to reach an agreement. In addition to instructing the Silk Factory Trade Association and issuing a copy of the settlement record to the relevant parties, it is also instructed to forward it to all workers to comply with. Due to this order, the six articles of the settlement record are listed below for all branch members to be aware of. The union also believes that the silk industry is in decline, and it is implementing painful wage cuts in the hope of labor-management cooperation. It is hoped that members of each factory will not neglect their duties due to the small wage cuts. This announcement must not be violated: (1) The wages of all silk factory workers in Shanghai shall be temporarily calculated at 85% of the original amount across all factories. (2) The silkworm moth subsidy that workers are entitled to shall still be issued at 45% of the original salary. (3) The wage increases and other benefits that workers are entitled to shall remain the same as before. (4) When the factory's business improves, the labor side may request the restoration of the original wages, but the wage reduction period will last until the end of May next year. (5) The treatment of workers in double cocoon factories is different from that in single cocoon factories, and any changes must be submitted to the government for approval. (6) This agreement shall take effect from November 1st.

Goldsmiths' Outworkers Demand Improved Treatment

Mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau Fails

The Labor Side Has Applied for Arbitration

The goldsmiths' outworkers in this city demanded that the employers improve their treatment. The executive committee of the labor union passed thirteen conditions and submitted them to the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation after being reviewed and approved by the Citizens' Training Association. The most important of these was the second condition, which stipulated that the wage rate for contract workers should be increased by 36% plus 30% of the employers' price list. The third condition stipulated that the wages of long-term workers should be increased by 30% of the original wages. The tenth condition stipulated that all tools used by the workers should be purchased by the employers. The twelfth condition stipulated that the meal allowance for contract workers should be six yuan per month. The Social Affairs Bureau convened several meetings, but the mediation could not proceed because both parties insisted on their positions. It was concluded that the mediation had failed. Later, the labor union sent representatives to negotiate with the employers, but to no avail. Therefore, yesterday, they submitted a petition to the Social Affairs Bureau to be forwarded to the Municipal Government, requesting arbitration.

Standing Committee Meeting of the National Federation of Commerce

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China held its 29th meeting of the Standing Committee yesterday afternoon at 4:00 p.m. Those present included Chairman Lin Kanghou, Standing Committee members Lu Guangxu, Chen Riping, Li Kuian, Zhang Yuquan, etc. The meeting was chaired by Lin Kanghou and recorded by Secretary Gu Huaibing. The agenda included the following: (1) Committee Member Li requested the government to allocate funds to aid silk merchants in Sichuan as a precedent. It was resolved to forward the request to the Ministry of Finance and Industry of the National Government for allocation. (2) The chairman proposed that the government had set a deadline of September 15th for the renewal of business registration licenses in various regions. The deadline has now passed, and countless people have not renewed their licenses due to the impact of the war. It was proposed that the government extend the deadline. It was resolved to pass the original proposal and request the government to implement it. Various important cases were then discussed, and the meeting was adjourned.

Local News II

Three Robbers Shot Dead on the Spot During a Robbery in Zhoujiazui Road

Six Robbers Commit Robbery, Three Dead, Two Injured

Bullets Fly, Detective Injured

Stray Bullets Injure a Woman and a Child

The Qian family at No. 375 Fuxing Lane, Zhoujiazui Road, was suddenly robbed yesterday morning at around 9:00 a.m. After receiving the news, the Harbin Road Police Station immediately dispatched armed Chinese and foreign detectives to the scene to surround and arrest the robbers. At that time, four robbers had already fled to the road and opened fire to resist arrest. The detectives returned fire, and the two sides exchanged more than forty shots. As a result, three robbers were shot dead on the spot. One foreign detective and one Chinese detective from the police station were injured, and two passers-by were also injured by stray bullets. Fortunately, they were not seriously injured. Afterwards, the detectives arrested two robbers in the house of the victim and took them to the police station for questioning.

Six Robbers Invade and Commit Robbery Qian Zugen, a Ningbo native, also known as Qizhang, jointly invested with others to open the Hecheng Tobacco Company on Oujia Road and served as the accountant. He lived at No. 375 Fuxing Lane, Zhoujiazui Road. Yesterday morning at 9:00 a.m., Qian had left for Ningbo on business. Suddenly, six robbers broke in through the front door. Two robbers stood guard downstairs, and the remaining robbers rushed upstairs. At that time, only Qian's wife, Chen, was in the room. She was shocked to see this situation, but had no way to resist. She had no choice but to let the robbers search and rob her, and the loss was about one hundred yuan.

Detectives Rush to Arrest Robbers Fuxing Lane is a private lane with only two Shikumen gates. Qian's residence is across from his neighbor's, and they can see each other. Therefore, the lane is very quiet. Passers-by did not know that the robbers were committing a robbery inside. Fortunately, two Chinese detectives from the Harbin Road Police Station were patrolling outside Fuxing Lane. Suddenly, they saw a woman running out of the lane and reporting to the police. The two detectives immediately summoned nearby patrol officers. One detective ran to the police booth and reported to the Harbin Road Police Station by telephone. Immediately, many armed Chinese and foreign detectives rushed to Fuxing Lane to arrest the robbers.

Three Robbers Killed on the Spot In an instant, the situation near Fuxing Lane suddenly became serious. Because four robbers had already rushed out of the lane gate and fled before the detectives arrived, they ran and opened fire on the detectives. The Chinese and foreign detectives also returned fire. For a time, gunshots crackled and sounded like a string of pearls. However, the guns fired by the robbers were mostly inaccurate and difficult to dodge. As a result, three robbers were shot in vital parts by the detectives and died on the road one after another. The places where the two robbers fell were not far from Fuxing Lane. One had already turned the corner and fled, but he could not escape death.

Detectives Shot and Injured When detectives and robbers exchanged fire, foreign detective Beinaite was shot in the right arm, and Chinese detective No. 2427 was also slightly injured. After being injured, foreign detective Beinaite was sent to Gongji Hospital for treatment and was not seriously injured. When Beinaite was not injured, he fired three shots and hit a robber. Another foreign detective, Shengtufute, also fired and hit a robber. The rest were shot and killed by Chinese detectives.

Stray Bullets Injure Two People Two people were also injured by stray bullets. One was Zhao Jiaxian, a fifteen-year-old apprentice at Lihua Sewing Company at No. 289 Zhoujiazui Road, a Ningbo native. He heard gunshots and went out through the back door to watch. A bullet flew and hit his left foot. The other was Chen Xia, a twenty-eight-year-old Yangzhou native and housewife of the tiger stove owner at No. 318 on the same road. She was watching idly at the door when a bullet hit her left leg. Both were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by a police car and were not seriously injured.

Supplementary Measures for Self-Defense by Merchants and Residents

Yuan Liang's Concern for Defense

Yuan Liang, the director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, pays special attention to winter defense. He has now drafted supplementary measures for self-defense by merchants and residents, which have been distributed to the heads of all districts and then forwarded to commercial organizations for distribution to all residents and businesses in the city. The supplementary measures are listed below: "Supplementary Measures for Self-Defense by Merchants and Residents": (1) In Shanghai, it is customary for residents to enter and exit through the back door. In the morning or evening, maids often leave the door ajar when going out to fetch water or buy groceries, which provides an opportunity for robbers to break in. Once they break in, they close the door, pull out weapons such as pistols, and prevent anyone from making a sound. They can only be allowed to rob and escape with the loot. Only then can the district office be notified, but the robbers have already fled far away. It is best to install foreign locks on the back doors. People leaving the house should close the door behind them and lock it themselves. When returning, they should use the key to open it. This is very simple and reduces the chance of robbers breaking in. It is indeed the best way to prevent them. (2) Most robberies occur around 7:00, 8:00, or 9:00 p.m. This is because it is customary for shops to close at this time and collect the day's sales at the accounting table to count and settle accounts. This provides an opportunity for robbers to break in and rob. If the shops close the door and settle accounts after closing, or if they can gradually store the day's sales upstairs during the day, the robbers will find it more difficult to climb the stairs and rob. (3) Installing an alarm bell is the most convenient way to report a crime. However, smaller shops may find it too expensive. If several shops can jointly set up one (such as the electric bell in a hotel that calls the tea room to drop the number plate), the cost to each shop will be reduced, and the effect will be great. (4) Robbers must scout the area for two or three days before committing a crime to see if there are any police officers nearby and how many people there are in the shops and residences. They carefully consider the escape route after the robbery before taking action. They never act rashly. If the shops and residents are attentive and observant, if they see any suspicious behavior, they should immediately report it to the district office so that they can pay attention. If a case occurs, it will be easier to catch them. (5) Residents and shops in Shanghai are accustomed to minding their own business and ignoring what is happening around them. Therefore, when robbers commit a robbery, they know that the neighbors only seek their own safety and will not help or report the crime. Only then do they dare to rob safely. If residents in the streets and neighborhoods can help each other and report the crime for each other, the robbers will have more concerns and will find it difficult to use their tricks. (6) Recently, many street robbery cases have occurred. The reason for this is that the money carried is not kept very securely and is seen by the robbers, resulting in losses. From now on, when shops send people to collect money, they should be carefully instructed to carry it discreetly along the way and not show it to the robbers. This can prevent the risk of being robbed.

Winter Defense Meeting of the Songbao Authorities

Qiu Minggu, the magistrate of Baoshan County, convened a special winter defense meeting at 1:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, attended by Shi Guanxi, the commander of the Lion Forest Fort of the Fortress Command, Zhang Han, the director of the Fourth District of the Wusong Water Police, and Wang Qingtao, Lu Fengpu, Yang Weixiong, the chiefs of the local defense corps, Qian Tianpeng, the director of the Construction Bureau, Wang Chuan, the section chief of the county government, Xue Ying, etc. The meeting was chaired by Qiu Minggu, and the following resolutions were immediately made: (1) The winter defense period will be from now until February 20th of the twentieth year. If necessary, it may be extended. (2) The joint defense measures for winter defense will be decided, and the implementation will be approved at the next meeting. (3) The Fourth District of the Water Police will assign additional police officers and deploy patrol boats to patrol various sand islands outside Songkou, such as Changxing Ruifeng Stone Island. (4) Strict household registration investigations will be implemented, and attention will be paid to the straw sheds in Jiangbei to prevent villains from mingling. In addition, there are several other proposals that will be submitted for discussion and public resolution at the next meeting.

Disputes over Water Charges After the Water Rate Increase

Since the Shanghai Waterworks Company increased its rates in September, the matter has not been resolved due to the opposition of various groups. However, the company insists on charging according to the increased amount, so the dispute is still raging. For example, Dou Yaoji Real Estate Company received a letter from the Shanghai Waterworks Company stating that it should send the bills for the six-percent water fee for the two locations on Beikai Road and Yangshupu in September so that it could be verified; otherwise, the water would be cut off on the 30th of this month. (The letter was printed with the words "Six-Percent Water Fee for Chinese Houses.") The company immediately prepared the water fee bills and the water fee bills for Aiduya Road and Longmen Road managed by it, and sent the six-percent water fee due along with the bills to the Shanghai Waterworks Company as usual. However, the Shanghai Waterworks Company actually returned the bills and the water fee and added the amount of the water fee increase on the bills. The company believes that the 30th day for cutting off the water is approaching, and the issue of the rate increase has not been resolved. If the Shanghai Waterworks Company actually cuts off the water at that time, causing various losses in life and property to the company's owners and tenants, it will hold the Shanghai Waterworks Company fully responsible. The company has already sent letters to the Shanghai Waterworks Company and the Chinese Ratepayers Association separately to inquire and appeal for support.

Wang Huiru Detained Again

Commits Two Cases in the French Concession

Judge Xu Approves the Transfer

Wang Huiru (also known as Wang Laowu), a twenty-nine-year-old Anhui native residing at No. 6 Xudong Lane, Tongfu Road, Huxi, was known for his wealth. Two years ago, he was involved in a kidnapping case and was arrested by the Xinzha Police Station. He was sentenced to eleven months in prison by the Provisional Court. Wang refused to accept the sentence and appealed, but the original judgment was upheld, and he was sent to the Xilao Prison in Tilanqiao to serve his sentence. He was released after his term expired last year. On the night before last at 9:30 p.m., Wang was arrested again for another case. At that time, Wang was passing through Nanjing Road when he was seen by a Chinese detective from the No. 38 French Concession Police Station, who reported to the No. 608 Indian sentry at that location, stating that the French police had recently captured kidnappers who had implicated Wang. Wang was detained and taken to the Laozha Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Xu Jiashi presided over the first criminal court for interrogation. Prosecutor Xu Mu also attended the court to perform prosecutorial duties. After Judge Xu asked Wang about his age, place of origin, and address, the police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated the case, saying that Wang had been arrested by detectives from the French Police Station at the Laozha Police Station last night. According to the detectives, Wang committed the crimes of attempted murder and supplying firearms to robbers in the French Concession. Therefore, the French Police Station requested the French Public Concession to issue an arrest warrant to transfer him. Upon investigation, the arrest warrant issued by the French Public Concession must be signed by the French Consul to be valid. However, the arrest warrant for Wang Huiru held by the French Police Station's foreign detective Lailier did not have the French Consul's signature or the Public Concession's seal. Therefore, it was not convenient to hand him over that night. Should Wang be allowed to be taken away now? Please let the judge decide. Now, the police station has brought the criminals who implicated Wang to court for questioning. Then, Gielier translated that the French Police Station had recently captured nine robbers, including Lu Lansheng, Duan Adi, and Lan Dagou. It had been found that these people had committed two robbery cases: (1) the robbery of property from the resident of No. 44 Lu Mei Road at 7:00 p.m. on September 30th; (2) the robbery of a pawnshop on Julai Road, during which the owner was shot in the right chest. According to the three robbers Lu, Duan, and Lan, the two pistols they used were borrowed from Wang Huiru. Therefore, the French Public Concession was requested to issue a warrant to arrest Wang. However, it was already late at that time, and the French Consul was not at the Public Concession, so the warrant could not be signed by the French Consul. Today is also a holiday for the French Public Concession. Although the warrant has been signed by the French Consul, the legal seal has not been affixed. Please allow the transfer. Then, according to Chinese detective No. 38, it was learned yesterday that Wang had opened room No. 438 at the Dongya Hotel on Nanjing Road. He went to investigate and saw that the guest in that room was registered as a Shi. Then, he saw Wang leaving the room and arrested him on the way. According to Lu Lansheng, he and Wang Laowu met in the Xilao Prison in Tilanqiao, introduced by a fellow prisoner Cao Guisheng. On the ninth day of August this year, Cao and others planned to rob Lu Mei Road. Because they did not have firearms, Cao suggested borrowing them from Wang. He and Jin Sheng went to Wang's house. At that time, Cao told Wang that he was fighting with someone and lacked pistols, so he came to borrow them. Wang went upstairs and brought out two pistols and handed them over. Cao took them out and went to rob Lu Mei Road. He fired one shot. Afterwards, he withdrew two hundred yuan from the account as a reward for borrowing the guns. According to Lan Dagou, he met Wang through Cao Guisheng's introduction in the Xilao Prison. When questioned, Wang Huiru said that he was only one wall away from Cao in prison, so he knew each other. Old prisoners in prison must bully new prisoners. After I got out of prison, I met Lan Dagou on Nanjing Road and was even borrowed ten yuan. This time, they must have been coerced by the French police to make false accusations. I have a lot of assets, so how could I do this illegal thing for two hundred yuan? If I had hidden weapons, there would be more than just two pistols. The police can search my house. The foreign detective of the French Police Station absolutely denied Wang's statement of being coerced and said that all the prisoners were there and could be questioned. Lan Dagou also claimed that his confession at the French Police Station was voluntary. Judge Xu then instructed that Wang Huiru be allowed to be handed over to the detectives of the French Police Station to be brought back and investigated.

Escapes by Climbing Over a Wall, Shot in the Right Shoulder

Surgery is Postponed, Hoping for No Changes

Zhou Changshun, courtesy name Changshan, the grandson of the late merchant Zhou Liantang, was kidnapped by bandits at the Jiangwan Racecourse on the morning of the 18th of last month. His temperature is over 38 degrees, and his pulse is slightly lower than when he arrived at the hospital. Fortunately, he is still conscious. Yang Jiabao and Wu Qiuxiang

Naked Man and Woman

The Sister-in-law Was Too Ruthless

The Father Forced Her Too Urgently

Xu Zhu, a woman from Suqian, 33 years old, lived in a flat behind the Huayuan Stone Bridge on Lan Nidu in Pudong. Her husband had worked as a dock coolie and had passed away six or seven years ago. Ms. Song initially vowed to remain a widow, relying on her husband's brother for support. However, her sister-in-law, Ge (32 years old), was very narrow-minded and often argued with Zhu. Zhu found the sarcasm and cold remarks unbearable, so she separated from her brother and sister-in-law in March of this year according to the lunar calendar, and went to the Longmao Warehouse to pick floral clothes to make a living. However, her wages were only four or five hundred cash per day, which was difficult to survive on. Forced to change her mind, she became intimate with Li Rongqing, a fellow villager. Li was 31 years old and worked as a cook. The two of them formed a small family at the east end of Xiaoyangjing Temple. But good things are often hard to come by. Zhu's father came to Shanghai from his hometown a few days ago and did not see his daughter's whereabouts, immediately arousing suspicion. He strongly accused her sister-in-law, Ge, of selling her off for a price, complaining incessantly. Ge, feeling wronged, was extremely angry. At three o'clock yesterday morning, she gathered many people and, without making a sound, broke into Zhu's bedroom, dragged Li Rongqing out of the bed, and tied up both him and Zhu with ropes, completely naked. Li shouted for help. Fortunately, a patrol officer from the Third District of the Public Security Bureau was passing by and went forward to inquire. The helpers scattered like birds and beasts. The two were untied, ordered to put on their clothes, and taken to the district along with Ge. Zhu's father, upon hearing this news, considered it a matter of face and immediately fled far away. After the district chief investigated the circumstances of catching the adulterers, he ruled that Ge should not have resorted to such base means and ordered her to be transferred to the court for disposal.

National Products Association Sends Telegram Requesting Exemption from National Product Advertising Tax

The China National Products Maintenance Association recently sent a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stating, "Respectfully to Chairman Ye of the Jiangsu Provincial Government in Zhenjiang: Respectfully reporting, we have recently received a letter from Cheng Ganqing, director of the Zhenchangxisu branch of the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company, stating: 'Respectfully reporting, we have investigated the Provincial Government Gazette of this year, March 15th, Issue No. 387, which published the approval of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's consultation, based on the Shanghai National Products Factory Association's request for exemption from the national product advertising tax. The Central Executive Committee approved the deliberation by the Ministries of Industry and Commerce, Finance, and Internal Affairs, deciding that all national product advertisements should be exempt from taxation, and consulted the provincial government to instruct its subordinate financial departments to investigate national product advertisements. If there are bureaus that collect taxes, they must be ordered to stop collecting them immediately to promote national products and conform to the decision. This is a case approved by the ministry and an order issued by the provincial government. Subordinate agencies should earnestly implement it. Our company's products are also a type of national product. Posting advertisements should be free of charge without any doubt. Both Jiangsu and Changzhou have already complied, but resistance has arisen in Wuxi and Zhenjiang, obstructing and resisting, disregarding the ministry's deliberation and the provincial order. Repeatedly arguing with reason has yielded no results, greatly hindering the promotion of national products and causing concern for the future of the industry. Compelled by circumstances, we have no choice but to petition your association to request the provincial government to investigate the established case and promptly order the counties of Wuxi and Dantu to no longer obstruct our company's national product advertisements. This would be greatly beneficial to the public.' Based on this, we respectfully note that promoting national products is an important policy of the party and the country. All things that benefit national products are earnestly implemented to achieve practical results. Now, the exemption of the national product advertising tax has been deliberated, approved, and ordered by the Ministries of Internal Affairs, Finance, and Industry, and published in the Provincial Government Gazette No. 387 of the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Jiangsu and Changzhou have already complied, but Zhenjiang and Wuxi are the only ones that do not comply with the laws and regulations and arbitrarily collect taxes, not only hindering the sales of national products but also affecting the credibility of the ministries and provinces. Our association, as a national product group, specially reports the situation by telegram. We respectfully request that your office investigate the established case and promptly order the counties of Wuxi and Dantu to comply with the order to exempt the national product advertising tax and no longer obstruct it, so that national products can be sold smoothly. We are eagerly anticipating this. Respectfully, Wang Jie'an, Wang Xingyi, and Wang Hanqiang, Standing Committee Members of the China National Products Maintenance Association, respectfully kowtow, with seal."

The Lights Outside the West Gate Suddenly Went Out

At 7:25 last night, the lights in the area of Zhaozhou Road, Laoximen (Old West Gate), and Fangbang Bridge in Nanshi (South City) suddenly went out. They were not repaired until after more than twenty minutes.

The Labor Hospital Held a Board Meeting Yesterday

The Shanghai Labor Hospital on Xiaoshadu Road held its sixth board meeting at 6 PM yesterday to discuss all matters of reform. Committee members Pan Gongzhan, Hu Hongji (representing Wu Heguo), Wu Bokang, Tang Demin, Zhang Yaoming, Wang Jingyang, Jin Wenqi, and Fan Shouyuan attended. The meeting also invited three standing committee members of the Finance Committee: Mr. Qin Runqing and Mr. Wang Yansong were present. Mr. Xu Jiqing was absent due to other commitments. Chairman Pan Gongzhan first reported that the hospital's expenses were huge and insufficient to cover them. He had previously submitted a document to the municipal government requesting a monthly subsidy of 2,000 yuan to maintain it. He has now received the municipal government's Instruction No. 6387, approving a monthly allocation of 1,000 yuan from the municipal government starting in January of the 20th year. He then reported the hospital's expenditure accounts for August and September and discussed soliciting donations from factory owners to expand and develop the hospital.

The YWCA's Huxi Women Workers' Club Opens

The Labor Department of the YWCA, considering the numerous factories in Huxi (West Shanghai), and the increasing number of female workers attending the Women Workers' Club previously established at Sanheli on Xiaoshadu Road, has established a new club at No. 4433 Yuqingli, Laobisheng Road, for the purpose of promoting the moral, intellectual, physical, and social development of female workers. The opening ceremony is scheduled for 2 PM on the 30th (Sunday), and Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, will be invited to speak. Students from the Labor Night School of Shanghai University and the Shanghai Jiangnan University String Ensemble will also perform to add to the enjoyment. Invitations have been extended to all sectors of society to attend. The Women Workers' Club will be open for visits from 4 PM to 6 PM that afternoon.
