A Barber Dies from Drunkenness

Qiao Changbao and Zhao Changshou, two barbershop employees at No. 2323 Yangshupu Road, drank alcohol in the shop the other day. As a result, Qiao became very drunk. His colleagues helped him to the back door to let the cool breeze sober him up. Unexpectedly, he collapsed and died shortly after. Someone reported it to the Yangshupu Police Station, which ordered Detective Chen Xikang to investigate. The body was moved to the Fei Lun Road autopsy station. Yesterday morning, Guo Huaipu, a prosecutor from the Special District Local Court, and a forensic doctor went to the station to conduct an autopsy. After taking the stand, he immediately accepted the complaint from the shop owner, Liu Chunlin, that Qiao Changbao had no family and that he would provide the coffin and burial. Mr. Guo then ruled that Qiao Changbao had died from excessive drinking and that the body could be buried by Liu Chunlin with a written guarantee.

Zhang Sang, a Woman Involved in a Robbery Case, Dies

Zhang Sang, a woman from Dongtai, was arrested by the Harbin Police Department and brought to the Special District Local Court for being involved in a robbery gang last summer. After interrogation, she was sentenced to three years in prison and sent to the women's prison. Recently, she suddenly suffered from stomach disease and weakness. She was sent to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment, but she died at 3 AM yesterday morning. The body was sent to the Fei Lun Road autopsy station. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Huaipu of the Special District Court and a forensic doctor went to the station to conduct an autopsy. It was determined that she had died of illness. As no relatives were found, the Putuo Benevolent Hall was ordered to provide the coffin and burial.

Old Li from Jiangbei Freezes to Death

This is a Gift of the Red Pill

In a shack at the Zhou family's residence at No. 63 Huatuan, Zhabei, there lies a dwelling of humble origin. However, those who dwell within were originally from wealthy families. Later, because of their involvement in the underworld, followed by the addiction to "red pills," their family property was reduced to nothing, and their bodies became weak. Those addicted to "red pills" inevitably die within three years, their blood dried up and their bones rotten. However, the individuals in this humble dwelling, according to the local security chief, are even more bizarre. They indulge in opium smoking daily on the straw mats in the shack. Because, apart from the opium pipe and lamp, they have nothing else of value. Clothes can be dispensed with, food can be foregone, but the opium must not be abandoned. These people are akin to those beyond the pale of civilization, and the authorities can do nothing about them. Recently, with the weather turning colder, lacking clothes and bedding, the underworld ghosts in the humble dwelling could not resist the wrath of heaven. Thus, yesterday, an old Li from Jiangbei, about 30 years old, froze and starved to death, his whole body turning yellow, a testament to the harm of opium addiction. However, as he had no family, the police station ordered the local security chief, Yan Liugen, to report the death to the Local Court for autopsy. Prosecutor Li and others arrived at the scene to conduct the autopsy, which confirmed the cause of death. The court ordered the benevolent hall to provide the burial.

Hu San's New Lawsuit for Stealing Land Outside of the Tan Mei Case

Hu Yongji (aka Hu San), who was accused of defrauding Tan Meiying (梅影) of a land deed in the case against Mei Fei (梅妃, i.e., Chen Junxia), has fled. Recently, he has been accused of illegally selling land belonging to Qian Guanquan, a villager. The villager has retained lawyers Zhang Chongding and Li Yuan to file a criminal lawsuit, requesting the Shanghai Special District Local Court to arrest Hu Yongji and the people currently building fences on the land for interrogation. The court approved the request and ordered the summons of the defendant Hu San, who has not yet appeared. The court session was held the other day, and the plaintiff's lawyers and the plaintiff Qian Guanquan were present in court awaiting instructions. Judge Ge Zhitan conducted the interrogation, but no debate was opened. As a result, witnesses must be summoned to court, and another court date will be set for further summons and interrogation.

Discharged Soldier Collapses and Dies

A discharged soldier collapsed and died inside the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) Railway North Station yesterday. He was Feng Jinshan, over 30 years old, from the 27th Regiment of the 14th Brigade of the Fifth Division. He had a travel permit. The railway police ordered the local security chief, Yan Fugen, to report the death to the Local Court for autopsy. Prosecutor Yang confirmed that he had died of illness, and the charitable hall provided the burial.

Zhong Wuliu Goes Missing, Search Underway

Zhong Wuliu (绍兴人之俗禮其父五十六歲養此子者名曰五六), a 14-year-old apprentice from Rongtaixiang Shop in Xue Alley, Huajinpailou, within the city walls, went missing at around 7 PM the other night. The next day, people were sent out to search for him, but he has not been found. Yesterday, the apprentice's appearance and the clothes he was wearing when he went missing were printed on leaflets with rewards. In addition to reporting the matter to the police station in charge, requesting that they keep an eye out for the apprentice's whereabouts, leaflets have been distributed to the public, requesting that they pay attention and look for him.

Vegetable Owner Robbed

At the corner of Baoshan Road and Zhongxing Road in Zhabei, there is a place with a public weighing scale. Every morning, those who have a license for the weighing scale (commonly known as "vegetable owners") bring a scale to weigh and buy vegetables from the villagers in the open air and then resell them to vegetable vendors, deducting a commission. However, the vegetable owners must advance capital, so they must carry a certain amount of cash every morning to advance the money. Yao A'gen, the owner of the weighing scale in that area, is very successful. Every morning, he must advance more than one hundred yuan for the vegetable capital, which attracts the covetousness of bandits. Yesterday morning (the 27th), just before dawn, when Yao was carrying cash to weigh and buy vegetables at the place, two bandits suddenly came, each holding a handgun, threatening Yao and others to be silent. They forcibly grabbed Yao's cash and paper money in his coat pocket, totaling more than one hundred yuan, and fled northward.

County Police Chief Transferred to Qingpu

Shen Jinghua, the police chief of Shanghai County, citing the difficulty of funding the county's public security, has sincerely submitted a request to the county government to approve his resignation. The other day, County Magistrate Yan forwarded it to the provincial department for review. According to reliable news from the county government, Police Chief Shen has been officially ordered to be transferred to Qingpu as the police chief. Once the successor is appointed, a notice will be sent to the county, and Police Chief Shen has ordered the departments to complete the handover so that he can transfer.

Dilapidated Houses Must Be Investigated Before Being Handled

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "For the information of the officials, the investigation and review of whether dilapidated houses should be ordered to be demolished and rebuilt is under the jurisdiction of the Public Works Bureau. This Bureau is not in a position to implement it immediately. In the future, if any of the aforementioned dilapidated houses are found, a report should first be submitted to this Bureau to request the Public Works Bureau to send personnel to conduct a clear inspection before handling it. In addition to the distribution, this notice is issued to the district chiefs for compliance and to instruct their subordinates to be informed."

Family of Deceased Sailor Zhou Jinquan Receives Money

For many years, when sailors and passengers on various Chinese and foreign ships died en route, their remains were thrown into the sea for burial at sea, as the ships did not have coffins and mortuaries. In addition, the journey was long, so burial at sea was the only option to prevent stench and affect the health of those on board. Later, the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong, with charity in mind, donated five or more coffins to each Chinese and foreign merchant ship. Then, donation boxes were set up on each ship, allowing passengers to freely donate and put money into the boxes to recover costs. Chinese and foreign passengers and crew members were very grateful, and many freely donated. However, in recent years, the same measures have not been taken on various Chinese and foreign cargo ships. Therefore, cargo ship crew members who die en route are still buried at sea. The China Seamen's Union has recently received a report from the family of Zhou Jinquan, a manager on the Guanghua Petroleum Company's ship柯派柯尔, stating that Jinquan died of illness near the "Shambit" oil field while the ship was traveling, and was buried at sea. They described the tragedy and requested that his estate be collected. In addition to the Seamen's Union assisting in collecting Zhou Jinquan's estate from the consulate, they deeply feel that the burial at sea of cargo ship crew members who die of illness is closely related to humanitarianism and the future. They have recently decided to contact the Tung Wah Hospital again, requesting that all Chinese and foreign cargo ships be treated in the same way as merchant ships. The following is a record of the Hong Kong Seamen's Association's report to the Seamen's Union and the committee's collection of Zhou Jinquan's estate: (1) The Hong Kong Seamen's Association reported, "Reporting matter: According to the report from the family of Zhou Jinquan, a manager on the Guanghua Petroleum Company's ship柯派柯尔, Zhou Jinquan died of illness near the Shambit oil field in September of this year and was buried at sea. However, he left behind unpaid wages and loans totaling more than ten pounds. The ship owner sent them to the local consul, who sealed and sent them to the US Consul in China, and there was also a letter from fellow workers such as Chen Huafen informing them to go to the consulate to collect the money. However, the deceased member's wife is young and his children are young and do not have the procedures. It is proposed that your association send someone to go with them to collect the money. Respectfully reporting for inspection and handling. Respectfully to the Union, Qiu Yaokuan, Committee of the Preparatory Office of the Hong Kong Branch." (2) The report of the Seamen's Union sending someone to collect the money on behalf of the family, "In accordance with the letter No. Zhengzi 4855, I was ordered to go to the British Consulate Maritime Affairs Office in this port at 2 PM on the 19th of this month with the deceased worker Zhou Jinquan's wife, Zhou Yang, and his father, Yang. I met Consul Beiyue, and I personally guaranteed that Zhou Yang was indeed Zhou Jinquan's wife. I then handed over the total cash estate of 346.7 yuan in national currency, and Zhou Yang signed for it. Respectfully reporting for inspection and filing. Li Zuyao, Secretary of the Seamen's Union, respectfully."

Tuition Fees of the Faculty of Law and Politics

The Shanghai Faculty of Law and Politics on Jin Shenfu Road in the French Concession, when Xu Qian was the principal, borrowed 85,000 yuan from a certain capitalist due to insufficient funds for building the school. Later, due to changes in the political situation, Xu Qian went abroad, and the principal was replaced several times. The creditor has repeatedly sought repayment of the loan from the current principal and school board, and the matter has been delayed until now without a solution. Therefore, the creditor has retained Lawyer Pan to submit a document to the Ministry of Education of the National Government, requesting that the school be ordered to settle the debt by the end of 1930. Because the creditor is in urgent need of funds, he has recently continued to request Lawyer Pan to draft another document to the Ministry of Education, requesting the revocation of the school's registration and permission to liquidate the school site to repay the debt if the matter is further delayed. It is unknown how the Ministry of Education will handle this matter.

ABC Underwear Factory Opens New Machines

The ABC underwear and fabrics woven by the China Underwear Weaving Factory are sold throughout the country and the South Seas Islands, and the demand often exceeds the supply. Therefore, this spring, 300 new-style weaving machines were added, and they have all been opened. There are also new-style sprayers to prevent the yarn and cloth from drying out, and new water heating machines are installed to send steam into the machine room, and then a motor is used to blow out warm air, making the room warm and even. The workers wear工衣自製 (self-made work clothes) of the factory, which is especially neat and uniform. The other day, the factory convened the third savings group to visit the factory, and they all praised it greatly. The savers believe that the factory uses savings to assist industry and uses industry to guarantee savings, so they are happy to invest in savings.

The Sin-French Pharmacy in this port has chosen a site to build a new branch in Hongkou, near the Hongkou Bridge. The new building has now been completed and has begun operations. It is also holding a one-month anniversary grand discount sale with gifts. In the past three days, customers have gathered, and business is booming.

Silk and Fur Union Price Reduction

Since the completion and opening of the four-story building of the Daxin Silk Bureau on Shilu (Stone Road), the scale has been grand, and the collection is rich. People from all walks of life recognize it as a large silk shop suitable for the modern era, and business is often prosperous. The Tianfa Fur Bureau in Paqiuchang has been a well-known large fur store in Shanghai for a long time. It has traveled to various ports over the years to purchase valuable furs and sell them at low prices. It is now heard that the two stores, in order to help all sectors of society solve the problem of winter clothing, have specially agreed to hold a joint silk and fur grand price reduction starting on November 29th. They are currently preparing, and it will soon be announced in the newspapers. This joint price reduction measure is still a pioneering effort in Shanghai, and it is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Worker Injured by Car

Yesterday afternoon at 6 PM, Jin Wenqi, an obstetrician, was driving his own car when a man resembling a worker, about 30 years old, wearing a blue cloth shirt and trousers, suddenly ran out from Nan Shi Da Ma Tou (Great Wharf). Although the driver caught a glimpse of him, it was too late to stop, and the car hit him, causing him to fall to the ground. The wheels then ran over his head, causing injury, brains splashed, and was extremely miserable. The patrol police heard about it and rushed to the scene, immediately detained the car, and sent the injured man to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment. It is said that the injury is severe and there is little hope of survival. Then the police took the driver back to the police station in charge for investigation.

Mutual Accusations Between Men and Women in a Sordid Society

Ms. Zhang Wei and Xu Songlin

Zhang Wei, a 29-year-old woman from Taizhou, yesterday, along with her cohabitant Xue Zhou, brought Xu Songlin to the Fourth District General Office to file a complaint. Director Jin interrogated the plaintiff, Ms. Zhang, who stated that her husband runs a wine shop at No. 6, Le'anfang, Mongol Road, and that around 10 PM the night before, she went out to fetch water. While passing by an alley, she was suddenly accosted by the defendant, Xu Songlin, who, along with two others, brandished weapons and threatened her. Xu held a knife to her chest, while the other two stripped off her original-colored woolen qipao, and together they robbed her of thirty dollars in banknotes, several small silver coins, and over ten copper coins she had on her. They then fled in different directions. She saw Xu escape into the Jinxi Inn nearby, but as it was already late at night, she didn't pursue them. Instead, she returned home to sleep and reported the incident to the police this morning, who arrested Xu and brought him to the office for investigation. Xue Zhou stated that Ms. Zhang was her tenant and that she was unaware of the robbery of clothes and money the night before. The defendant, Xu, a 32-year-old from Baoshan, who lives at the Jin Chang Inn on Mongol Road, stated that he had become acquainted with Ms. Zhang through Zhou's introduction in August of this year. He had spent a considerable amount of money on her, but Ms. Zhang turned out to be fickle and had recently found another lover. He was so angry that he took back the clothes he had given her, but he denied taking any money. The Director, after reviewing the testimonies, noted that the case involved robbery with weapons, and the testimonies differed. He ordered that the case be transferred to the bureau for further investigation.

News from Various Labor Unions

Anglo-American Tobacco Factory Union: The tin foil factory of the Anglo-American Tobacco Factory in Pudong suddenly and without reason dismissed a large number of workers, twenty in total, last Friday, causing dissatisfaction among all workers. The union has reported the matter to the Citizens Training Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau, who have sent representatives to negotiate. The factory's attitude is firm, leaving no room for negotiation. The workers, on the other hand, have made three demands to the factory: (1) Comply with the final mediation of the senior representatives, giving one month's severance pay for each year of work, with more years receiving more. (2) If the factory needs to add workers in the future, the twenty workers who were unjustly dismissed this time must be given priority for re-employment. (3) Replace the Western foreman, who is not allowed to beat workers, and apologize to the union. The factory has not accepted the above three demands, and the situation has remained unresolved for many days. The union believes that such a delay is unacceptable and has scheduled the fifth second representative assembly at 6 PM on the 25th of this month to discuss assistance measures in order to resolve the matter. 114 representatives attended, with Zhang Sheng, a representative from the Municipal Party Department, attending to provide guidance. The chairman was Chen Peide, and the recorder was Sun Xiaozhu. Formalities were observed, and the report was omitted. Matters discussed: (1) How to assist the tin foil factory workers who were dismissed. Resolution: All workers will donate two small silver coins per month for three months. After three months, the union will solicit donations from the outside world to prepare for a long-term struggle to awaken the factory. (2) Are there any amendments to the demands of the tin foil factory workers? Resolution: No need for amendments. However, wages during the workers' strike period must be paid by the factory. (3) List of candidates to organize an economic preparation committee to assist dismissed tin foil factory workers. Resolution: Li Laifa, Ying Qipei, Ren Kunda, Zhang Hefang, Chen Peide, Hu Songxiang, Gu Ruofeng, Bao Yangzhou, Zhang Chuncai, Fei Keguang, Zhang, Jin Zifang, and Dong Aosheng were elected, totaling 13 people, and Chen Peide was appointed as the convener of the charity. (4) Year-end bonuses for workers should be negotiated with the factory to be issued at the end of the solar year. Resolution: The board of directors will negotiate with the factory. (5) Increase the allowance for the resident doctor Wang Depei. Resolution: Increase the monthly allowance by five dollars. Finally, Zhang Sheng, a representative from the Citizen Training Committee, provided guidance, and the meeting adjourned.

Pharmaceutical Workers Union: The third first joint meeting of directors and supervisors was held yesterday, chaired by Zhao Zhenhui. Formalities were observed, and the standing committee members of the directors and supervisors and the heads of various departments were elected as follows: (1) The union should elect five standing committee members of the directors. Zhao Zhenhui, Qian Xuanmin, Cai Maohuai, Fang Qinghe, and Ye Zuren were elected as standing committee members of the directors, with Zhao Zhenhui as the chairman. (2) The union should elect one standing committee member of the supervisors. Fang Qingjian was elected as the standing committee member of the supervisors. (3) The union should elect the heads of various departments. Zhao Zhenhui was elected as the head of the general affairs department, Qian Xuanmin as the head of the organization department, Fang Qingjian as the head of the mediation department, Fang Qinghe as the head of the training department, Cai Maohuai as the head of the publicity department, and Ye Zuren as the head of the accounting department. The accounting department was divided into two sections, with Fang Yihong as the member of the expenditure section and Ying Jinde as the member of the collection section.

Tongchong Shipping Barge Industry Union: A group leader meeting was held the day before yesterday (7 PM on the 26th). Formalities were observed. Chairman Gu Peirong reported that since the establishment of the union, if the members of various industries do not unify regarding the issue of non-members working, how should it be handled? After deliberation by the group leaders, it was resolved: (1) Non-members shall not enjoy the 2% commission; all 2% commissions shall be enjoyed by members who have joined the union. (2) If non-members do not listen to the command of the group leaders, they shall be reported to the executive committee of the union for handling. (3) In the future, members shall not be absent from meetings without reason. The meeting adjourned after discussion.

Cotton Weaving Workers Union: The sixth first board meeting was held yesterday, with Yu Kunqiu publicly elected as chairman. Formalities were observed. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, and then the following resolutions were discussed and passed: (1) Establish an audit committee. Resolution: Xu Xingxing, Liu Zuofang, Xu Ajin, and Wang Guisheng were appointed as audit committee members. (2) How to subsidize the union's financial difficulties. Resolution: All membership fees owed in the past shall be canceled. Starting from November, personnel shall be dispatched to collect membership fees. (3) The union's request to revise conditions and increase wages. Resolution: Submit to the Social Affairs Bureau for handling. (4) The union hires Gong Zhijian as a voluntary secretary and Wei Qin as a voluntary clerk. (5) How to solicit non-members who have not joined the union. Resolution: Personnel shall be dispatched to solicit them, and they shall be given a deadline to join the union. Those who fail to register with the union by the deadline will not be guaranteed. The meeting adjourned after discussion.

Ship Wood Industry Union: The tenth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees was held yesterday, chaired by Ye Xianggao. Resolutions: (1) Feng Dao's letter of resignation. Resolution: Due to the urgency of union affairs, the resignation was not approved, and a letter will be sent to retain him. (2) A small number of foremen do not comply with the agreement. Resolution: In accordance with the Municipal Government's No. 1057 directive, a lawsuit will be filed directly in court. (3) The two accounts books submitted by Liu Alai and Wang Qinsheng from Chedaijiao should be audited. Resolution: Li Ruiyu and Zhang Liqin were immediately appointed to audit them. (4) Official documents submitted to the superior authorities should be signed by the responsible person. Ye Xianggao and Lin Jingchu were publicly elected to sign. The rest was omitted.

Guanshengyuan Workers Union: The twelfth executive committee meeting was held yesterday, chaired by Xu Jichang. Resolutions: (1) The application for membership of six employees, including Wen Tang, Lu Jingmin, Lu Qicheng, Cai Dechen, Yu Shaoan, and He Qi, was reviewed and approved. The company will be notified by letter. (2) Relocation of the union headquarters to No. 30, Heng'anfang, Zhaozhou Road. Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky is overcast and uncertain, and there may be fog and rain in the Yangtze River basin. There is a gentle cyclone here, caused by the low pressure in Jiangxi moving northeast-east. The wind direction in the Yangtze River basin and Shandong is uncertain. Also, within the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 62.6, and the lowest was 42.3. On the same day last year, the highest was 63.1, and the lowest was 28.0.

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor: In a news item published in your newspaper's local news column on the 17th of this month, it stated that Cheng Zhang, a staff member of the Yutai Pawnshop on Fangbang Road, absconded with gold jewelry worth six or seven thousand dollars, and after the pawnshop reported the incident to the Second Branch of the First District of the Public Security Bureau, it was discovered that he was hiding in the Nanyang Hospital in Xiaonanmen, Nanshi. The director of the branch ordered detectives Li Dingyuan and police officer Cheng Rufu to arrest him. We were shocked to read this. The total value of the ornaments lost from our pawnshop was only slightly more than three thousand. Rufu was also present at the time as one of the representatives of the pawnshop, so he was also at the scene. Now your newspaper mistakenly identifies him as a police officer, which is inconsistent with the original facts. We are afraid that the outside world will misunderstand the truth, causing misunderstandings. We are writing to inform you and ask you to investigate and publish a letter to correct this matter. Sincerely, Cheng Rufu, Yutai Pawnshop, November 20th. To the Editor: I have read the news item in your newspaper's local news column on the 26th about welcoming Mr. Chu Minyi. There are some minor errors, so I am writing to correct them as follows: (1) Shao Ru-xin is mistakenly written as Shao Ru-sheng. (2) The Huzhou fellow villagers' separate banquet is mistakenly written as the Huzhou Fellow Villagers Association's separate banquet. Please publish this letter in the letter column to clarify the facts. Thank you very much. Sincerely, the Shanghai Preparatory Office for Welcoming Mr. Chu, the representative of the National Government participating in the Belgian Exposition, November 27th.

Youth Forum

Jiaotong University's Swimming Program

Jiaotong University has very well-equipped swimming facilities. After losing the swimming competition to Jinan University this year, they felt that it would be difficult to wash away the shame without making an effort to practice. Therefore, there is a plan to heat the swimming pool. The method is to install hot water pipes at the bottom of the swimming pool to keep the water temperature in the pool at around 15 degrees Celsius. In the cold winter, electric heaters must be installed around the pool, so that even in extremely cold weather, practice can continue without interruption. After the school's swimming team has obtained this special equipment, it has become even more diligent. It is specifically stipulated that Mondays, Wednesdays, and Fridays are the team members' practice periods. At that time, the captain will call the roll. Those who are not absent for a semester will be rewarded by the director of physical education. Those who are absent once will be given a verbal warning by the captain, twice a written warning, and three or more times, the captain will ask the director of physical education to issue a written warning. If they still ignore it, they will be deemed to have withdrawn from the team, and the student's physical education score will be deemed failing. The team members are able to abide by the regulations and work hard. Since February, there has never been an absentee, so the results have greatly improved. The achievements of each team member are described below:

The Ye Brothers: Ye Hang is the elder brother, and Ye Wu is the younger brother. The two Ye brothers are the most diligent in practice among all the team members. The elder Ye's 200-meter crawl can already be swum within the time of the Jiangda record, and the posture is excellent. Given time, there will be amazing records. The younger Ye is a long-distance swimmer. Now the school's Master He has taught him the latest Long Distance Crawl method used in the United States. The Ye brothers practice purely and are making progress every day. The 3,000 meters can be swum in 33 minutes, which is almost the same as the Jiangda record.

Mr. Ling Chongju: Mr. Ling is the nephew of Ling Hongxun, the former president of the school and current director of the Longhai Railway Engineering Bureau. He is naturally skilled in swimming, and he grew up in Guangdong, accompanied by rivers and seas. Since being selected as a team member, he has also worked very hard. The 200-meter breaststroke can be swum in one minute and twenty-seven seconds, breaking the Jiangda record.

The above three gentlemen are the brightest members of the school's swimming team. They are now under the guidance of designated lecturers, and it is also heard that the school's physical education department believes that swimming is especially important in physical strength. In order to strengthen the team members' physical strength, the school doctor has been specially invited to formulate ten rules for the team members' daily life and diet to be followed. The general idea of the rules is to set the time for daily life, how to control the diet, etc. In addition, the team members' meals are also borrowed by the school authorities to provide rich nutrition.

A Glimpse of Fudan Publications

— Bin

There are no fewer than a thousand students, male and female, at Fudan University. There are indeed many who have made achievements in literary research. Therefore, in the past two years, small publications that focus on literature and art have been popular for a while, such as "Modern Literature," "Asahi," "Humor," and "Contemporary Literature." At the beginning of their publication, they attracted the attention of the Shanghai literary world. After all, due to economic reasons, they were discontinued one after another after publishing a few issues. However, its achievements, in the history of the publishing world, cannot be completely buried. However, it is a pity that it was discontinued soon after it was published. Now, publications on literature and art and other topics have sprung up like bamboo shoots after a rain. Because the publication period is short, perhaps outsiders are still unaware of them. Now I will briefly describe their content for the benefit of fellow enthusiasts.

A. Hongliu This is the most violent attack on Proletarian literature. Although only the inaugural issue has been published, it has attracted the attention of students and the outside world, because some of the articles in it are very logical in discussing the decline of Proletarian literature. It makes a complete criticism of past general Proletarian publications, and obviously contains deep insights. It is extremely familiar with the current publishing world and is by no means a casually produced work of scolding. An article criticizing "Literature Lectures" objectively criticizes each article in it, and of course points out hundreds of mistakes, because the so-called Marxist writings only deceive the blindly following youth. Those with a little deep knowledge will never be tempted by their mad rantings. Therefore, in today's era of clearing up thoughts, such critical texts are very necessary for their production. At least, its power can point out a correct ideological path for young people who love literature and art. At the same time, the publication also expresses its approval of nationalist literature, but their attitude has not been clearly revealed. A publication always has its own goals, and it must not engage in ambiguity. Only with this point, we consider it a regret.

B. Huoban This is a purely literary publication, including novels, poems, essays, etc. Each work has an upward consciousness and holds a dissatisfied aim for Proletarian literature, but they have not published a complete critical article, but only one issue. Or if this article is found later, at the same time, this is also what we hope for.

C. Journal of the Department of Sociology This is a bimonthly publication edited by the publishing department of the Alumni Association of the Department of Sociology. Two issues have been published. The content is extremely rich. Writers are students and teachers working together. This publication is highly recommended for those who study social sciences. The main points of these two issues are excerpted below: 1. Ying Chengyi's "What is Truth?" Xiao Yuan's "Principles of Group Conflict," Chen Yuchun's "Relationship between Instinct, Habit, and Wisdom," Wang Zaiqin's "Animal Sociology," Li Hongsheng's "On Modern Social and Cultural Phenomena," Chen Peisen's "Research on Allied Strikes," Mao Qi's "Fudan University's Plan to Investigate the Income of Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers." The arguments in each article are mostly precise and correct, which is commendable. It is very gratifying to be able to read powerful treatises in such a small publication. It is heard that the third issue may also be published soon, including an article by Mr. Ying Chengyi, "The Truth and Falsehood of the Theory of Social Evolution," which is very noteworthy for us.

D. The Importance and Implementation of Journalism Education This is the recent work of Director Xie of the Department of Journalism, published by the Journalism Society. The content discusses the importance of journalism education, especially in our country. It is really necessary to promote this education. The implementation focuses on the curriculum organized by the Department of Journalism of this school, and cites the facilities of journalism departments in various countries for comparison. This is entirely Director Xie's detailed development of his experience. If national universities were to open journalism departments, this book could be used as a reference, because such works have not yet been found in domestic publications. The pricing is also very low. Scholars who study journalism or education can also purchase and read it, and can really obtain considerable help from it.

There are many other publications in preparation, which will be reported to readers later. In short, such a wide range of publications as Fudan University is worthy of attracting the attention of outsiders. That is to say, the above types belong to the brilliant side in terms of content, which is also worthy of our praise.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

The Second Issue of Vanguard Monthly

— Gao Wei

Published by Modern Bookstore

Since the publication of the "Inaugural Issue of Vanguard Monthly," the activity in the Chinese literary scene has become even more profound. This is an inevitable result and nothing to be surprised about. Today, the inclination of young people who love the arts towards the nationalist literary movement is a fact formed by objective conditions. Therefore, they are eagerly reading and accepting it. Now the second issue has been published, and the table of contents includes: Fu Yanchang's "The Literary Movement Centered on National Consciousness," Chen Baoyi's "An Overview of the Development of Western Painting in Japan," Zhu Yingpeng's "Chinese Painting and Nationalism," Yang Minwei's "Chinese Ceramics and Nationalism," Li Zanhua's short story "Change," Zheng Bo's novel "Xiuer" (continued), and Tiran's short translation "The Night Watchman," and Li Jinfa's novel translation, "The End of Beijing," are all powerful works.

Fu Yanchang's "The Literary Movement Centered on National Consciousness," although only a short article of about a thousand words, is very pertinent and says what others have not said. The author bluntly states, "The literary works with national consciousness as the central idea, the most without status in the world, have to be pushed to us Chinese as the first. What we Chinese lack most in common sense is this national consciousness." This is so true. If Chinese people had national consciousness, they would never be ridiculed as a heap of loose sand. Because with national consciousness, there will be激昂 group action. Group action is always𤍠情的 and beneficial to the nation. At present, what our Chinese literature lacks is this point. The encirclement of traditional thought really makes us feel sad. Therefore, if we want to promote a powerful idea that benefits the Chinese people to the general public, then this idea must be the opposite of traditional thought in order to gather together for a unified action for the nation.

...It doesn't matter how profound the thought is, as long as it can be utilized, it is good. What we Chinese people need now is just a national consciousness that can be utilized.

In our group's opinion, literary works should be a manifestation of life under the group, and definitely not a separate action for individuals to enjoy alone. Chinese literary works should be used by all Chinese people, and we will definitely not allow the free thought of everyone being muddy while I alone am clear. Someone said that as long as it is a Chinese literary work, it will inevitably tend towards nationalism - I say, just look at traditional literature and you will know this is wrong. The Chinese literary scene is now full of anti-nationalist traditional thought and literary works with individual-centered thought. The Chinese people who have been propagandized are therefore a heap of loose sand, or a pile of unusable garbage. The Chinese people have no group strength and no status in the international community. These are all the results of the propaganda promoted by literary works.

Arise, propagandize, let us engage in literary works and strive upwards with national consciousness as the central idea.

Chen Baoyi's "An Overview of the Development of Western Painting in Japan" is a history and current situation of the Japanese Western painting scene. The author's motivation for writing this article is seeing that although the Western painting movement in our country has a history of several years, it is still stagnant in tangible and intangible ways. Compared with Japan, it is truly incomparable. Therefore, at the beginning, the author pointed out the situation of the Chinese Western painting scene in detail, and explored from all aspects, believing that for our society and for our culture, it seems that we should not stop the upward trend of art, and should not stop engaging in artistic creation, in order to show a broad effect. In order to do this, we should all have mutual understanding, and individuals should seek their own upward progress, which seems natural. The individual upward progress of art will naturally become one of the cooperation of the whole. Although now is a time of practical difficulties, if we hold a sincere heart and a clear understanding, then when the time comes, we may break through various difficulties. At this time, we should work hard to forge ourselves, and work together to build, the Chinese Western painting scene and increase the brilliance of our new culture." Next, it mentions the development history and current situation of Western painting in Japan, and discovers that they are both Eastern nations, how brilliant they are, and what our situation is like. Can we not feel ashamed and reflect? They are steadfastly building art careers in many difficulties. This situation, seen as a national characteristic, also has outstanding advantages. As for the author's narrative of historical facts, it is very detailed and can be used as our reference.

But since painting is also one of the arts, what Baoyi said lacks theoretical elaboration and guidance on practical work. What is the relationship between Chinese painting and nationalism? Then we read Zhu Yingpeng's "Chinese Painting and Nationalism." This is worthy of our attention, especially for people who generally study art. Generally speaking, Chinese painting has its own special style, special techniques, special materials, and is different from the painting of all nations in the world. It is unique. Therefore, in the eyes of people with general concepts, they will think that these are our national art. Just add the banner of nationalism, and it will be considered our nationalist painting. The author expresses that "this general concept is the current thorn in the nationalist literary and art movement." Therefore, first determine the prerequisite principle, and then discuss whether the inherent Chinese painting is produced from the living consciousness formed from the standpoint of the nation, and whether it has assumed the mission of "for the nation" for its own national consciousness. Therefore, it is studied in two aspects, one is the issue of thought, and the other is the issue of technique and style. Thought can be divided into two types, one is feudal thought, and the other is world-weary thought. The painting theory of feudal thought can be represented by Lu Shiheng, Cao Zhi, Xie He, Zhang Yanyuan, Gu Yanwu...etc. They are fundamentally products of feudal politics. The painting theory of world-weary thought can be represented by Guo Zhao, Wang Wei, Zhang Huai, Su Shi, Ni Zan, Dong Qichang, Shi Tao, etc. Secondly, discuss the techniques and styles. Generally speaking, thought always occupies the main point in art, and painting is the same. Thought can produce techniques and styles. In other words, techniques and styles are just a tool of expression. We can prove this with German expressionism, French purism, Italian futurism, and Russian primitivism. Therefore, the techniques and styles of inherent Chinese painting have become decorative and freehand due to the relationship between feudal thought and world-weary thought. These two traditional thoughts and the inherent Chinese painting dominated by the techniques and styles they produce cannot be recognized as national art. The author also sees from the aspect of hindering national progress that inherent Chinese painting does not pay attention to the performance of life. Those painters are conquered by these two kinds of unified thoughts and are absolutely not responsible for life. The self-proclaimed noble freehand painters will never give up their cynical attitude, and will never plan for the lives of the people. Therefore, according to the "Manifesto of the Nationalist Literary and Art Movement," we should rise up and work hard to eliminate it. At the same time, future Chinese painting "should no longer seek a way to survive in the degenerate old painting, but should have new understanding and creation. Fundamentally, it should be confirmed that art and life must be integrated, and even more should burst out with blazing sparks and surging springs from the national purpose." And in the performance, special attention should be paid to: A. National shame and suffering, B. National primitive legends, C. National struggle history, D. National actual life, E. Praise of material civilization. This can also be said to be the mission of Chinese painting. "We need new understanding, new emotions, and new thoughts for painting, and at the same time we need new materials, new techniques, and new styles as tools for all expressions. These new techniques and styles should be created by the painter's efforts." Ah, people who are generally engaged in painting, don't just blindly drill on the old dead road. Please use your creativity. The author also establishes the minimum principles of our painting techniques and styles: (1) Take sketching as the basis, (2) Take healthy development as the standard of human beauty, (3) The composition must be rigorous, (4) Make with a deliberate attitude, (5) The color is mainly bright and𤍠烈, (6) Pay attention to lines, (7) Pay attention to the expression of movement.

Yang Minwei's "Chinese Ceramics and Nationalism" first explains the relationship between ceramics and the Chinese nation, and then narrates a brief reading of the history of Chinese ceramics, from the earthenware of the primitive era to the ceramics of the Han Dynasty, the celadon porcelain of the Jin Dynasty... the ceramics of the Yuan Dynasty, the ceramics of the Ming Dynasty, and the ceramics of the Qing Dynasty, which is very detailed. Finally, it discusses the efforts that the Chinese nation should make for ceramics. To save the declining trend of the ceramic industry, first reorganize the old factories across the country, and second, concentrate the spirit and strength. "In this way, the salvation of Chinese ceramics is equal to saving the Chinese nation itself. Therefore, the creation of ceramics by the Chinese nation is a creation with doctrine, a creation of nationalist ceramics. The art of ceramics of the Chinese nation is an art with doctrine, an art of nationalist ceramics. The ceramics of the Chinese nation have the original driving force centered on nationalism and nationalist art, and they will definitely be able to restore the glorious history of ceramics in the near future, not only to restore, but also to create. This major mission should be borne by the Chinese nation itself."

"Change" is a work by Li Zanhua standing on the主

Page 24

righteous literary and artistic standpoint. The climax of the story is the terror of the communists encountered by a village. Women, children, and the elderly flee in cries. Originally, they were all doing their business quietly, but there was a big robbery of killing and arson without mercy, making innocent villagers taste the pain of, "The night is so dark, the mountain road is so rugged, where to go, the line of people is stunned." What kind of happiness is this? The author focuses on the mother of Wax Plum and the pig in the Wax Plum's pen. The pig that the mother of Wax Plum cares about day and night, thinking that this is a sum of money for the New Year, which has been arranged long ago, but she has to give it up because of the escape. And when she looks back at her home, it has been surrounded by a blood-red fire. What should be this kind of instinctive sadness? Therefore, from the reflection of the mother of Wax Plum, it fully expresses a profound sense of potential. In terms of branch skills, this creation is indeed very considerate, very natural, and there is no trace of artificiality. Moreover, the situation of the farmer's life is depicted very powerfully. As for the tightness of the structure, it is difficult to find loose places. In the creation of nationalist literature and art, this "Change" can be said to be a powerful expression.

"The Night Watchman" is the original work of Amelia Aharonian. According to the author's introduction, Aharonian is the most famous Armenian novelist of the twentieth century, and also a tireless warrior for the freedom and security of the nation. We can find Aharonian's melancholy and激昂 style in this article. What kind of feeling will his inner consciousness give the reader? The night watchman is a rebel against fate. He absolutely does not admit fate. If human beings have such a thing as fate, it is tantamount to saying that human beings have no intention of struggling. But how does he have this unique consciousness? He has his story. He told the people in the coffee shop that he had struggled with fate himself, and had overcome fate and defeated fate. In the hands of the violent, the enemy, because of the strong feeling of anti-fate, he even turned the violent to death. He had such an awareness at that time. He saw that the crane first pecked the snake, and then turned around and was entangled to death by the snake. But maybe it was the author's parable, "The struggle between the snake and the stork also caused a change in my heart. I have never heard anyone say that a snake can strangle a stork. The stork was originally the snake's mortal enemy, the incarnation of the snake's god of fate. However, today, how can its god of fate not be able to control it? Is it difficult for God to allow even a poisonous snake to become a stork's, unfair carnivorous, allow our fate to be solved by this Celt? No, I said to myself, my previous thoughts were wrong. A person must work hard to find a way out." Later, he finished telling his own story, and made the whole room people could not help but fluctuate "In many voices in the home, people heard the call for freedom," the whole article is very tense, we can say that it is a successful short story.

"The End of Beijing" is the original work of Pierre Loti of France, writing the tragedy of the Eight-Nation Alliance, which made me feel really thrilling after reading it, thinking of our nation being trampled on by foreign nations, and all kinds of insults, can not be indignant, and reflect, hoping to save the crisis of our nation. At the same time, general literary and art writers should also realize that we have not used such materials ourselves, but foreigners have already used them before us. Are you not ashamed? Alas, the end of Beijing is probably also a symbol of the end of China. This article has not been completed in this issue.

Looking at this issue of "Vanguard Monthly," we can think that it is substantial, but don't be complacent because of this. We still need to follow the "call" of progress and actively rush forward. My introduction ends here, as for the many essences, please readers analyze it themselves.

The Manchuria-Mongolia Question

— Nanxin

Compiled by Hua Qiyun

Manchuria and Mongolia occupy an important position in our China. Although they are located on the periphery, they are profound and significant for industrialists. However, this point has been valued by foreigners, that is, the Japanese's attention to our Manchuria and Mongolia, as long as there is a new problem in this area, their newspapers will definitely write about it greatly and promote it doubly, hoping to arouse the extra attention of people across the country and stimulate their interest in research, so that general readers can have a kind of attention role with the newspaper. Therefore, there are those who collect history books to examine the origin of this Manchuria-Mongolia question, those who write articles to criticize its current situation, and those who set it as speculation to predict its future. Soon, articles on this type of new question spread throughout the country. This is in terms of its general people, as for its government, there are those who send special commissioners to Manchuria and Mongolia every year to investigate the industry, and those who investigate the rich resources. The number of people they send is really no less than dozens of hundreds. From this, it can be seen that they pay attention to Manchuria and Mongolia, but it is close to our people. However, books on Manchuria and Mongolia can be regarded as abundant in Japan, and in our China they are really as rare as morning stars, and not valued by people. Then, the publication of this book recently compiled by Mr. Hua has considerable significance and value.

The whole book is about more than 100,000 words, and it can be regarded as the most abundant masterpiece for studying the Manchuria-Mongolia question. The content is divided into three chapters: 1. Geography of Manchuria and Mongolia, 2. Economy of Manchuria and Mongolia, 3. Diplomacy of Manchuria and Mongolia. Manchuria and Mongolia originally refer to the three northeastern provinces and Mongolia, because of the natural situation and artificial reasons, there are often special names such as South Manchuria, North Manchuria, Inner Mongolia, and Outer Mongolia. This has a close relationship with diplomacy. Based on this point, the author starts by explaining the geography of Manchuria and Mongolia. Everyone can know that Manchuria and Mongolia have vast land and sparse population, but the products are the richest and the transportation is the most developed, especially the prosperous trade. This, the author has a chapter on the economy of Manchuria and Mongolia, and at the same time, it can make us understand the development of Manchuria and Mongolia today. Of course, the diplomacy of Manchuria and Mongolia is even more important. There is an emphasis on the relationship between the two countries, such as China and Russia, and China and Japan, and there is a common relationship with the countries, such as the United Kingdom, the United States, France, and Germany. Therefore, the author divides the chapter on the diplomacy of Manchuria and Mongolia into three chapters: China and Russia and Manchuria and Mongolia, China and Japan and Manchuria and Mongolia, and the countries and Manchuria and Mongolia, to add detailed descriptions, so that we can understand the truth more easily after reading it.

The geography of Manchuria and Mongolia is described in two chapters, (1) Geography of Manchuria, which explains the location and name of Manchuria, "Manchuria is bounded by the mouth of the Ussuri River, the Songacha River, and Lake Khanka to the Russian Maritime Province in the east, by the Tumen and Yalu Rivers to the Japanese Korean peninsula in the south, by the Heilongjiang River to the Russian Amur Province in the north, by the Ergun River to the Russian Transbaikal Province in the northwest, and by the Yellow Sea and the Bohai Sea in the southwest. The total area is about 373,700 square miles." Although this describes the border and area of Manchuria, it can make us understand the relationship between Japan and Russia in Manchuria. At the same time, it has such a vast area. If our people never operate it, what kind of crisis will the future contain? In other words, the Japanese's attention to our Manchuria can show a glimpse of their ambition. (2) South Manchuria and North Manchuria. This is divided into two major parts according to the natural situation of Manchuria. North Manchuria has a vast area and a sparse population. The mountains and fields have the most trees. South Manchuria has a small area, but is rich in cultivated land. The population is large and the soil is fertile. However, after the Russo-Japanese War of Jia Chen, the two sides concluded the "Treaty of Portsmouth", and then stipulated that the Manchurian Railway south of Changchun was ceded to Japan. By the first year of the Republic of China, Japan and Russia concluded the second secret agreement, then dividing Manchuria south of Changchun as Japanese and Manchuria north of Changchun as Russian. Here, the sphere of influence of the two countries can be seen. Like this kind of historical fact, we need to know it in detail. (3) Kwantung State is also an important territory in the area, occupying the southern part of the Liaodong Peninsula and the nearby islands. Therefore, the author specially puts forward a separate discussion. The geography of Mongolia first explains the location and name of Mongolia, and then describes Inner Mongolia and Outer Mongolia, and lists detailed tables of their district names, tribe names, number of banners, and provinces included, so that readers can easily understand. Again, it describes eastern Mongolia and eastern Inner Mongolia, quoting Lin Daoyuan's "Study of the Situation of Eastern Mongolia" to explain its area in more detail.

The economy of Manchuria and Mongolia is described comprehensively. 1. Agriculture of Manchuria and Mongolia, A. Cultivated land and agricultural products of Manchuria and Mongolia, B. Soybeans, sorghum, millet, millet, wheat and miscellaneous grains, C. Cotton, tobacco leaves, sugar beet and peanuts, D. Orchards, E. Tussah silkworm industry, 2. Mining of Manchuria and Mongolia, A. Rich mineral products of Manchuria and Mongolia, B. Coal mines, C. Iron mines, D. Gold mines, E. Other minerals, 3. Forestry of Manchuria and Mongolia, 4. Animal husbandry of Manchuria and Mongolia, 5. Fisheries of Manchuria and Mongolia, 6. Currency of Manchuria and Mongolia, 7. Transportation of Manchuria and Mongolia, 8. Trade of Manchuria and Mongolia. The author has explanations and charts in each section, and the sub-sections are well-organized, which is one of the most complete chapters describing its economic scope.

The diplomacy of Manchuria and Mongolia is divided into three parts, upper, middle and lower. The upper part is China and Russia and Manchuria and Mongolia, 1. From Russia's eastward invasion to the Sino-Japanese War, 2. From the Sino-Japanese War to the Russian Revolution, 3. From the Russian Revolution to the establishment of the Russian Association, 4. From the establishment of the Sino-Russian Association to the present, the middle part is China and Japan and Manchuria and Mongolia, 1 From the Sino-Japanese War to the outbreak of the European War, 2. From the declaration of war against Germany to the establishment of the Japanese Tanaka Cabinet, 3. From the establishment of the Japanese Tanaka Cabinet to the present, the lower part is the powers and Manchuria and Mongolia. This part is more important than the previous two parts, so that we can understand the origin of the current precarious situation in Manchuria and Mongolia, and can arouse the vigilance of the people of the country and jointly seek strategies to save this declining situation. At the same time, the related relationship of these three countries can also be seen at a glance. The four appendices are especially for reference.

Mr. Hua's book is detailed in the preparation of Manchuria and Mongolia, which is worthy of attention.
